----- FILE: /opt/scalp/dp.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ---------- CONFIG ----------
ROOT="/opt/scalp"
DUMP_DIR="${ROOT}/dump"
mkdir -p "$DUMP_DIR"
TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')"
OUT="${DUMP_DIR}/scalp_full_${TS}.txt"
MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB="${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB:-512}"

# ---------- GIT ENV ----------
[ -f /etc/scalp.env ] && . /etc/scalp.env
: "${GIT_USERNAME:?}"
: "${GIT_TOKEN:?}"
GIT_BRANCH="${GIT_BRANCH:-main}"
GIT_EMAIL_USE="${GIT_EMAIL:-${GIT_USERNAME}@users.noreply.github.com}"
REMOTE_URL="https://${GIT_HOST:-github.com}/${GIT_OWNER:-$GIT_USERNAME}/${GIT_REPO:-Scalp}.git"

# ---------- HEADER ----------
{
  echo "# ===== SCALP PROJECT DUMP ====="
  echo "# $(date -u +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC')"
  echo "# Root: $ROOT"
  echo
  echo "========== TREE =========="
} > "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    sz=$(stat -c%s "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    mt=$(stat -c%y "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo unknown)
    printf "%-80s %12s %s\n" "$f" "$sz" "$mt" >> "$OUT"
done

{
  echo
  echo "========== FILE CONTENT =========="
} >> "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    echo -e "\n----- FILE: $f -----" >> "$OUT"
    cat "$f" 2>/dev/null >> "$OUT" || true
done

# ---------- DATABASE STRUCTURE (finale complète) ----------
{
  echo
  echo "========== DATABASE STRUCTURE =========="
} >> "$OUT"

for DB_PATH in /opt/scalp/project/data/*.db; do
  [ -s "$DB_PATH" ] || continue
  echo -e "\n----- DATABASE: $DB_PATH -----" >> "$OUT"

  {
    echo "-- TABLES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null || echo "(locked or unreadable)"
    echo

    for T in $(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null); do
      echo "[TABLE: $T]"
      sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "PRAGMA table_info($T);" 2>/dev/null || true
      echo
    done

    echo "-- VIEWS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='view' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no views)"
    echo

    echo "-- INDEXES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='index' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no indexes)"
    echo

    echo "-- TRIGGERS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='trigger' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no triggers)"
    echo
  } >> "$OUT"
done

# ---------- GIT PUSH ----------
cd "$ROOT"
git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree >/dev/null 2>&1 || git init -q .
git config user.name "$GIT_USERNAME"
git config user.email "$GIT_EMAIL_USE"
git remote get-url origin >/dev/null 2>&1 || git remote add origin "$REMOTE_URL"

git add -f "$OUT"
git commit -m "dump ${TS}" || true
AUTH_URL="https://${GIT_USERNAME}:${GIT_TOKEN}@${REMOTE_URL#https://}"
git push -f "$AUTH_URL" HEAD:"$GIT_BRANCH"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/OB_collect.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_U="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect.log"

echo "[$(date)] OB_COLLECT START" >> "$LOG"

# load universe
mapfile -t UNIVERSE < <(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_U" "SELECT instId FROM universe;")

# transform AAVE/USDT → AAVEUSDT_UMCBL
convert_inst() {
    echo "${1//\//}"_UMCBL
}

while true; do
    for inst in "${UNIVERSE[@]}"; do
        sym=$(convert_inst "$inst")

        URL="https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/candles?symbol=${sym}&granularity=60"
        JSON=$(curl -s "$URL")

        # Check valid response (must be array)
        if echo "$JSON" | jq -e '.[0]' >/dev/null 2>&1; then
            ts=$(echo "$JSON" | jq -r '.[0][0]')
            o=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][1]')
            h=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][2]')
            l=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][3]')
            c=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][4]')
            v=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][5]')

            sqlite3 "$DB_OB" <<SQL
INSERT INTO ohlcv_1m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
VALUES("$sym", $ts, $o, $h, $l, $c, $v)
ON CONFLICT(instId, ts) DO UPDATE SET
    o=excluded.o,
    h=excluded.h,
    l=excluded.l,
    c=excluded.c,
    v=excluded.v;
SQL

        else
            echo "[$(date)] ERR $sym Invalid JSON: $JSON" >> "$LOG"
        fi
    done

    sleep 1
done

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

# Sécurité: vérifier que la base n'est pas verrouillée
if lsof "$DB" | grep -q ob.db; then
  echo "❌ ob.db en cours d'utilisation. Ferme les processus avant d'agréger."
  lsof "$DB"
  exit 1
fi

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;

-- (Optionnel mais recommandé si non créés) Index pour accélérer l'agrégation
-- CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_1m_inst_ts ON ohlcv_1m(instId, ts);

-- Nettoyage 3m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;

-- Agrégation 1m -> 3m sans fonctions analytiques (compat SQLite 3.37)
WITH g AS (
  SELECT
    instId,
    (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts3,
    MIN(ts) AS ts_min,
    MAX(ts) AS ts_max,
    MAX(h) AS h,
    MIN(l) AS l,
    SUM(v) AS v
  FROM ohlcv_1m
  GROUP BY instId, ts3
)
INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m(instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
SELECT
  g.instId,
  g.ts3 AS ts,
  (SELECT o FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_min) AS o,
  g.h,
  g.l,
  (SELECT c FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_max) AS c,
  g.v
FROM g;

-- Vérification
SELECT '3m' AS tf, COUNT(*) AS rows, datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts
FROM ohlcv_3m;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
clear
echo "===== DASH B_SIGNALS ====="
echo

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 6 10 10 10 8 20
SELECT instId   AS COIN,
       side     AS SIDE,
       reason   AS REASON,
       price    AS PRICE,
       atr      AS ATR,
       ROUND(score_B,2) AS SCORE_B,
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS TS_LOCAL
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
LIMIT 20;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY GLOBAL -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers off
.mode column
SELECT
  'BUY :'  || COUNT(*)  FILTER (WHERE side='buy')  || '   ' ||
  'SELL :' || COUNT(*)  FILTER (WHERE side='sell') AS "SIGNALS"
FROM signals_B;

SELECT 'LAST SIGNAL :' || instId || ' ' || side || ' ' ||
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM signals_B ORDER BY ts_signal DESC LIMIT 1;

SELECT 'AVG AGE (s): ' ||
       printf("%.1f",AVG((strftime('%s','now')*1000-ts_signal)/1000.0))
FROM signals_B;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY BY COIN -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 8 8 10
SELECT instId AS COIN,
       COUNT(*) AS N,
       ROUND(AVG(score_B),2) AS AVG_SCORE,
       datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS LAST_TS
FROM signals_B
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY N DESC
LIMIT 15;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY BY REASON -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 12 8 8 10
SELECT reason AS REASON,
       COUNT(*) AS N,
       ROUND(AVG(score_B),2) AS AVG_SCORE,
       datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS LAST_TS
FROM signals_B
GROUP BY reason
ORDER BY N DESC
LIMIT 15;
SQL

echo "-----------------------------"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_gate_counter.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db
DB_A=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
DB_U=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

echo "===== B GATE COUNTER ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_A' AS A;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_U' AS U;

.headers on
.mode column

-- Gate#1: candidats (universe ∩ feat_1m frais)
WITH uni AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId FROM U.universe
),
feat_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_feat
  FROM feat_1m GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
g1 AS (
  SELECT u.instId, f.ts_feat
  FROM uni u JOIN feat_latest f ON f.instId=u.instId
  WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - f.ts_feat) <= 120000
),
-- Gate#2: ctx frais
ctx_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_ctx
  FROM A.ctx_a_latest GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
g2 AS (
  SELECT g1.instId, g1.ts_feat, c.ts_ctx
  FROM g1 LEFT JOIN ctx_latest c ON c.instId=g1.instId
  WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - c.ts_ctx) <= 300000
),
-- Gate#3: signal produit <= 600s
sig_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts_signal) AS ts_sig
  FROM signals_B GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
)
SELECT
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM U.universe)                      AS universe,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g1)                              AS g1_feat_ok,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g2)                              AS g2_ctx_ok,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g2 JOIN sig_latest s USING(instId)
     WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - s.ts_sig) <= 600000) AS g3_sig_ok;

DETACH DATABASE A;
DETACH DATABASE U;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_join_verify.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "=== VERIFY A(ctx) ↔ B(feat) normalized join ==="
sqlite3 /opt/scalp/project/data/b.db <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db' AS A;
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT 
  (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT REPLACE(instId,'/','')) FROM feat_1m) AS feat_coins,
  (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT REPLACE(instId,'/','')) FROM A.ctx_a_latest) AS ctx_coins,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (
      SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM feat_1m GROUP BY 1
  ) f
  JOIN (
      SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM A.ctx_a_latest GROUP BY 1
  ) c USING(inst)) AS join_matches_norm;
DETACH DATABASE A;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_sources_probe.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db
DB_A=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
DB_OA=/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db
DB_U=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

echo "===== B SOURCES PROBE ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_A'  AS A;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_OA' AS OA;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_U'  AS U;

.headers on
.mode column
.width 11 8 8 8 19 10 19 10 19 10

WITH uni AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId FROM U.universe
),
feat AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_feat
  FROM feat_1m
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
ctx AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_ctx
  FROM A.ctx_a_latest
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
sig AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts_signal) AS ts_sig
  FROM signals_B
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
oa5 AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_oa5
  FROM OA.ohlcv_5m
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
mix AS (
  SELECT u.instId,
         f.ts_feat,
         c.ts_ctx,
         o.ts_oa5,
         s.ts_sig
  FROM uni u
  LEFT JOIN feat f ON f.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN ctx  c ON c.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN oa5  o ON o.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN sig  s ON s.instId=u.instId
)
SELECT
  instId AS COIN,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_feat)/1000.0) AS age_feat_s,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_ctx )/1000.0) AS age_ctx_s,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_oa5)/1000.0) AS age_oa5_s,
  datetime(ts_feat/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_feat,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_feat) <= 120000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_feat,
  datetime(ts_ctx/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ctx,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_ctx ) <= 300000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_ctx,
  datetime(ts_sig/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_sig,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_sig ) <= 600000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_sig
FROM mix
ORDER BY age_sig_s IS NULL, gate_feat DESC, gate_ctx DESC, age_feat_s DESC
LIMIT 25;

.print ''
.print '--- GATES SUMMARY (Universe only) ---'
.headers off
SELECT 'Universe coins: ' || COUNT(*) FROM U.universe;
SELECT 'feat_1m fresh <=120s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM feat_1m f
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(f.ts)) <= 120000
);
SELECT 'ctx_a_latest fresh <=300s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM A.ctx_a_latest a
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(a.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(a.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(a.ts)) <= 300000
);
SELECT 'signals_B updated <=600s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM signals_B s
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(s.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(s.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(s.ts_signal)) <= 600000
);

DETACH DATABASE A;
DETACH DATABASE OA;
DETACH DATABASE U;
SQL

echo
echo "Hint: si seuls 1-2 coins sont 'OK' en feat/ctx, c'est amont (OA/A). Si feat/ctx OK mais sig OLD, c'est B_signals."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_B_output.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/check_B_output.log"
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"
stamp(){ printf "[%s] %s\n" "$(date '+%F %T')" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }

stamp "=== CHECK B MODULE OUTPUT ==="

if [[ ! -s "$DB" ]]; then
  stamp "❌ Base b.db absente ou vide"
  exit 1
fi

# Liste les vues et tables
stamp "--- STRUCTURE ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | tee -a "$LOG"

# Vérifie la présence de signaux
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | grep -qw signals_B; then
  stamp "--- DERNIERS SIGNAUX (signals_B) ---"
  sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -header -column "
  SELECT instId, side, reason, score_B,
         datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_signal
  FROM signals_B
  ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
  LIMIT 10;
  " | tee -a "$LOG"
fi

# Vérifie la vue signals_for_open
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | grep -qw signals_for_open; then
  stamp "--- SIGNAUX POUR OPEN (signals_for_open) ---"
  sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -header -column "
  SELECT instId, side, reason, score_B,
         datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_signal
  FROM signals_for_open
  ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
  LIMIT 10;
  " | tee -a "$LOG"
else
  stamp "⚠️  signals_for_open absente"
fi

# Vérifie les vues de résumé
for view in v_signals_coin_overview v_signals_summary v_signals_latest; do
  if sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | grep -qw "$view"; then
    stamp "--- ${view} ---"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -header -column "
    SELECT * FROM $view LIMIT 5;
    " | tee -a "$LOG"
  fi
done

stamp "=== FIN CHECK B OUTPUT ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_a_health.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_OA="/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"
DB_A="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/a_health.log"

{
  printf "\n===== HEALTH CHECK [A + OA] %s =====\n" "$(date '+%F %T')"

  echo -e "\n--- [OA] Fraîcheur TF 5m ---"
  sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_OA" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT 
  COUNT(DISTINCT instId) AS instruments,
  ROUND((strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)),1) AS age_s,
  datetime(MAX(ts/1000),'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_candle
FROM ohlcv_5m;
SQL

  echo -e "\n--- [A] Fraîcheur ctx_a_latest ---"
  sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_A" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT 
  COUNT(*) AS ctx_rows,
  ROUND((strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)),1) AS age_s,
  datetime(MAX(ts/1000),'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM ctx_a_latest;
SQL

  AGE_OA=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OA" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_5m;")
  AGE_A=$(sqlite3 "$DB_A" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ctx_a_latest;")

  if (( ${AGE_OA:-999999} > 300 )) || (( ${AGE_A:-999999} > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️  Données trop anciennes → relance scalp-oa.service et scalp-a.service"
    systemctl restart scalp-oa.service || true
    systemctl restart scalp-a.service || true
  else
    echo "✅  Données fraîches : OA et A dans les 5 dernières minutes."
  fi
} >>"$LOG" 2>&1

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ctx_sources.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== CHECK CTX SOURCES (A→B) ====="

# --- feat_1m : table brute de features
echo
echo "[feat_1m : derniers contextes et âges]"
sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/b.db "
WITH latest AS (
  SELECT instId, ctx, MAX(ts) AS ts
  FROM feat_1m
  GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT instId, ctx,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
       (strftime('%s','now') - ts/1000)/60.0 AS age_min
FROM latest
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

# --- v_ctx_a_latest : vue du contexte produit par A_ctx.py
if sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/a.db ".tables" | grep -q "ctx_a_latest"; then
  echo
  echo "[ctx_a_latest : contextes depuis A]"
  sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/a.db "
  SELECT ctx, datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
  FROM ctx_a_latest
  ORDER BY ts DESC
  LIMIT 10;"
else
  echo
  echo "[ctx_a_latest : vue absente]"
fi

# --- v_ctx_latest (si existante)
if sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/a.db ".tables" | grep -q "v_ctx_latest"; then
  echo
  echo "[v_ctx_latest : contextes consolidés]"
  sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/a.db "
  SELECT ctx, datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
  FROM v_ctx_latest
  ORDER BY ts DESC
  LIMIT 10;"
fi

# --- doublons avec ou sans slash
echo
echo "[Doublons slash / sans slash]"
sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/b.db "
WITH base AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS baseId, instId, COUNT(*) AS c
  FROM feat_1m
  GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT baseId,
       GROUP_CONCAT(instId) AS variants,
       SUM(c) AS total
FROM base
GROUP BY baseId
HAVING COUNT(*) > 1
ORDER BY total DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "===== END CHECK ====="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_feat_freshness.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -e
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
echo "=== FEATURE FRESHNESS $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') ==="
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -separator "|" "
SELECT '1m' AS tf,
       COUNT(*) AS rows,
       datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts,
       round(strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts)/1000,1) AS age_s
FROM feat_1m
UNION ALL
SELECT '3m', COUNT(*), datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
       round(strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts)/1000,1)
FROM feat_3m
UNION ALL
SELECT '5m', COUNT(*), datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
       round(strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts)/1000,1)
FROM feat_5m;
"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ob_ohlcv.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/check_ob_ohlcv.log"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"

stamp(){ printf "[%s] %s\n" "$(date '+%F %T')" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }
sql(){ sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" "$@"; }

# --- Vérifs de base ---
if [[ ! -s "$DB" ]]; then
  stamp "❌ ob.db absent ou vide: $DB"
  exit 2
fi

has_tbl(){ sql "SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='$1';" | grep -q 1; }

stamp "=== CHECK OB OHLCV ==="

stamp "--- Tables présentes (sqlite meta) ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | tee -a "$LOG"

for TF in 1m 3m 5m; do
  TBL="ohlcv_${TF}"
  if has_tbl "$TBL"; then
    stamp "--- $TBL ---"
    sql -header -column "PRAGMA table_info($TBL);" | tee -a "$LOG"
    sql -header -column "
      SELECT COUNT(*) AS rows,
             datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts
      FROM $TBL;
    " | tee -a "$LOG"
    sql -header -column "
      SELECT instId,
             MIN(ts) AS ts_min,
             MAX(ts) AS ts_max,
             datetime(MIN(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS dt_min,
             datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS dt_max
      FROM $TBL
      GROUP BY instId
      ORDER BY ts_max DESC
      LIMIT 5;
    " | tee -a "$LOG"
  else
    stamp "⚠️  Table absente: $TBL"
  fi
done

stamp "=== DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ofcr.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OPEN="/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_FOL="/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_CLO="/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_REC="/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"

echo "===== CHECK O-F-C-R PIPELINE ====="

check_table() {
    local name="$1"
    local db="$2"
    local table="$3"
    local tscol="$4"

    if ! sqlite3 "$db" ".tables" | grep -qw "$table"; then
        printf "%-9s → %s ❌ (missing table: %s)\n" "$name" "$name" "$table"
        return
    fi

    local count last
    count=$(sqlite3 "$db" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    last=$(sqlite3 "$db" "
        SELECT 
            printf('%02dh%02dm%02ds ago',
                (strftime('%s','now')-MAX($tscol/1000))/3600,
                ((strftime('%s','now')-MAX($tscol/1000))%3600)/60,
                ((strftime('%s','now')-MAX($tscol/1000))%60)
            )
        FROM $table;
    " 2>/dev/null || echo "00h00m00s ago")

    if [[ "$count" =~ ^[0-9]+$ && "$count" -gt 0 ]]; then
        printf "%-9s → %s ✅  (%s recs, last=%s)\n" "$name" "$name" "$count" "$last"
    else
        printf "%-9s → %s ✅  (0 recs, last=00h00m00s ago)\n" "$name" "$name"
    fi
}

# --- CHECK PIPELINE (tolérant) ---
check_table opener   "$DB_OPEN" "trades_open_init" "ts_open"
check_table follower "$DB_FOL"  "trades_follow"    "ts_update"
check_table closer   "$DB_CLO"  "positions_closed" "ts_close"
check_table recorder "$DB_REC"  "trades_recorded"  "ts_close"

echo ""
# --- LAST OPEN ---
echo "--- LAST OPEN ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_OPEN" -header -column "
SELECT instId, side, entry, sl, tp,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS opened
FROM trades_open_init
ORDER BY ts_open DESC
LIMIT 5;
" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no table trades_open_init)"

echo ""
# --- LAST FOLLOW ---
echo "--- LAST FOLLOW ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_FOL" -header -column "
SELECT instId, side, entry, sl, tp, pnl,
       datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS updated
FROM trades_follow
ORDER BY ts_update DESC
LIMIT 5;
" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no table trades_follow)"

echo ""
# --- LAST CLOSE ---
echo "--- LAST CLOSE ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_CLO" -header -column "
SELECT instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason_exit,
       datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS closed
FROM positions_closed
ORDER BY ts_close DESC
LIMIT 5;
" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no table positions_closed)"

echo ""
# --- LAST RECORD ---
echo "--- LAST RECORD ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_REC" -header -column "
SELECT instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason,
       datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS closed
FROM trades_recorded
ORDER BY ts_close DESC
LIMIT 5;
" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no table trades_recorded)"

echo "===== END CHECK ====="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ofr.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
echo "===== CHECK O-F-R STATUS $(date '+%H:%M:%S') ====="

check_db() {
  local label=$1 db=$2 table=$3 ts_col=$4
  [[ -f "$db" ]] || { echo "$label ❌ no DB"; return; }

  local count ts_last age_s age_hms
  count=$(sqlite3 "$db" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  ts_last=$(sqlite3 "$db" "SELECT MAX($ts_col) FROM $table;" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  [[ -z "$ts_last" || "$ts_last" == "0" ]] && ts_last=0

  local now=$(($(date +%s%3N)))
  age_s=$(( (now - ts_last) / 1000 ))
  if (( age_s < 10 )); then s="✅"
  elif (( age_s < 60 )); then s="⚠️"
  else s="❌"
  fi
  age_hms=$(printf "%02dh%02dm%02ds" $((age_s/3600)) $(((age_s%3600)/60)) $((age_s%60)))
  echo "$(basename "$db") → $label $s ($count rows, last=$age_hms ago)"
}

check_db "FOLLOWER" "$DATA/follower.db" "trades_follow" "ts_update"
check_db "CLOSER"   "$DATA/closer.db"   "trades_close"  "ts_close"
check_db "RECORDER" "$DATA/recorder.db" "trades_record" "ts_record"

echo "====================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
echo "=== OHLCV FRESHNESS $(date '+%F %T') ==="
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -column -header <<'SQL'
SELECT
  '1m' AS tf,
  COUNT(*) AS rows,
  datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts,
  ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM ohlcv_1m
UNION ALL
SELECT
  '3m',
  COUNT(*),
  datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
  ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1)
FROM ohlcv_3m
UNION ALL
SELECT
  '5m',
  COUNT(*),
  datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
  ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1)
FROM ohlcv_5m;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_pipeline_full.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "===== PIPELINE FULL CHECK ====="

DBO=/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db
DBF=/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db
DBC=/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db
DBR=/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db

echo
echo "--- [O] trades_open_init ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBO" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', sl) AS sl,
       printf('%.2f', tp) AS tp,
       status,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS open_time
FROM trades_open_init
ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [O] → [F] vue v_for_follower ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBO" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', sl) AS sl,
       printf('%.2f', tp) AS tp,
       ctx,
       printf('%.2f', score_B) AS score_B
FROM v_for_follower
ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [F] trades_follow ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBF" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', sl) AS sl,
       printf('%.2f', tp) AS tp,
       printf('%.2f', pnl) AS pnl,
       status
FROM trades_follow
ORDER BY rowid DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [F] → [C] vue v_for_closer ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBF" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', sl) AS sl,
       printf('%.2f', tp) AS tp,
       ctx
FROM v_for_closer
ORDER BY 1 DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [C] positions_closed ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBC" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', exit) AS exit,
       printf('%.2f', pnl) AS pnl,
       datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS close_time
FROM positions_closed
ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [C] → [R] vue v_for_recorder ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBC" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', exit) AS exit,
       printf('%.2f', pnl) AS pnl
FROM v_for_recorder
ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- [R] trades_recorded ---"
sqlite3 -readonly -header -column "$DBR" "
SELECT instId, side,
       printf('%.2f', entry) AS entry,
       printf('%.2f', exit) AS exit,
       printf('%.2f', pnl) AS pnl,
       datetime(ts_record/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS record_time
FROM trades_recorded
ORDER BY ts_record DESC LIMIT 10;
"

echo
echo "--- COHERENCE SUMMARY ---"
echo "[O→F] => trades_open_init -> trades_follow"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBO" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trades_open_init;"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBF" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trades_follow;"
echo
echo "[F→C] => trades_follow -> positions_closed"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBF" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trades_follow;"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBC" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM positions_closed;"
echo
echo "[C→R] => positions_closed -> trades_recorded"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBC" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM positions_closed;"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBR" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trades_recorded;"

echo
echo "✓ Contrôle complet terminé"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_pipeline_timing.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DBD=/opt/scalp/project/data

printf "\n===== PIPELINE HEALTH CHECK =====\n"

echo -e "\n--- [B] Derniers 3 signaux ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/b.db" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, side, reason, ROUND(score_B,2) AS score_B,
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_signal
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
LIMIT 3;
SQL

echo -e "\n--- [O] Dernières 3 ouvertures ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/opener.db" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, side, entry, sl, tp, status,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open
FROM trades_open_init
ORDER BY ts_open DESC
LIMIT 3;
SQL

echo -e "\n--- [F] Suivis actifs (2 meilleurs / 2 pires) ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/follower.db" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, side, printf('%.4f', pnl) AS pnl,
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_open)/1000.0,1) AS duration_s,
       datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update, status
FROM trades_follow
WHERE status='active'
ORDER BY pnl DESC
LIMIT 2;
SELECT instId, side, printf('%.4f', pnl) AS pnl,
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_open)/1000.0,1) AS duration_s,
       datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update, status
FROM trades_follow
WHERE status='active'
ORDER BY pnl ASC
LIMIT 2;
SQL

echo -e "\n--- [C] Dernières 3 clôtures ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/closer.db" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, side, printf('%.4f', pnl) AS pnl,
       reason_exit, datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close
FROM positions_closed
ORDER BY ts_close DESC
LIMIT 3;
SQL

echo -e "\n--- [R] Derniers 3 enregistrements ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/recorder.db" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, side, printf('%.4f', pnl) AS pnl,
       datetime(ts_record/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_record
FROM trades_record
ORDER BY ts_record DESC
LIMIT 3;
SQL

echo -e "\n✓ Contrôle pipeline terminé"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_post_opener.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DBD=/opt/scalp/project/data

echo "===== CHECK POST-OPENER PIPELINE ====="

# --- 1. État général des tables ---
for db in opener follower closer recorder; do
  FILE="${DBD}/${db}.db"
  [[ -f "$FILE" ]] || { echo "❌ $db.db absent"; continue; }
  echo -e "\n--- ${db^^}.DB ---"
  sqlite3 -readonly "$FILE" ".tables"
done

# --- 2. Derniers enregistrements ---
echo -e "\n--- [O] trades_open_init ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/opener.db" -header -column "
SELECT instId,side,entry,sl,tp,status,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open
FROM trades_open_init
ORDER BY ts_open DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

echo -e "\n--- [F] trades_follow ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/follower.db" -header -column "
SELECT instId,side,pnl,status,
       datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_update
FROM trades_follow
ORDER BY ts_update DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

echo -e "\n--- [C] positions_closed ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/closer.db" -header -column "
SELECT instId,side,pnl,reason_exit,
       datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close
FROM positions_closed
ORDER BY ts_close DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

echo -e "\n--- [R] trades_record ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/recorder.db" -header -column "
SELECT instId,side,pnl,reason_exit,
       datetime(ts_record/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_record
FROM trades_record
ORDER BY ts_record DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

# --- 3. Vérification cohérence OFCR ---
echo -e "\n--- [COHERENCE O→F→C→R] ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DBD/closer.db" <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db' AS F;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db' AS O;
SELECT c.instId,
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM O.trades_open_init WHERE instId=c.instId) AS n_open,
       (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM F.trades_follow WHERE instId=c.instId) AS n_follow,
       COUNT(*) AS n_close
FROM positions_closed c
GROUP BY c.instId
ORDER BY c.ts_close DESC
LIMIT 20;
DETACH DATABASE F;
DETACH DATABASE O;
SQL

echo "===== END CHECK ====="

ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM signals_for_open) AS n_signals_for_open,

  (SELECT datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') FROM signals_B) AS last_ts_B,
  (SELECT datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') FROM signals_for_open) AS last_ts_for_open;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ticks_flow.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# === CHECK TICKS FLOW (T_TICKS PIPELINE) ===
# Vérifie que les ticks arrivent régulièrement et sont frais (< 15s)
# Logs détaillés : /opt/scalp/project/logs/check_ticks_flow.log

LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/check_ticks_flow.log"
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
THRESHOLD=15 # secondes max entre tick et maintenant

mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"
stamp(){ printf "[%s] %s\n" "$(date '+%F %T')" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }

stamp "=== CHECK TICKS FLOW $(date '+%F %T') ==="

if [[ ! -s "$DB" ]]; then
  stamp "❌ Base t.db absente ou vide"
  exit 1
fi

# Vérifie la table ticks
if ! sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" ".tables" | grep -qw ticks; then
  stamp "❌ Table ticks absente dans t.db"
  exit 1
fi

# Extraction des 5 derniers ticks
stamp "--- DERNIERS 5 TICKS ---"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" -header -column "
SELECT instId,
       lastPr,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS tick_time,
       printf('%.1f s', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts)/1000.0) AS age_s
FROM ticks
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 5;
" | tee -a "$LOG"

# Vérifie la fraîcheur globale
AGE_MAX=$(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0 FROM ticks;")
if (( ${AGE_MAX%.*} > THRESHOLD )); then
  stamp "⚠️  Dernier tick trop vieux (${AGE_MAX%.*} s > ${THRESHOLD}s)"
else
  stamp "✅ Ticks frais (${AGE_MAX%.*} s)"
fi

# Vérifie la diversité (nb de coins actifs)
COUNT_COIN=$(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT instId) FROM ticks;")
stamp "Coins actifs : $COUNT_COIN"

if (( COUNT_COIN < 5 )); then
  stamp "⚠️  Peu de coins actifs → problème de flux ?"
else
  stamp "✅ Flux multi-coin OK"
fi

stamp "=== FIN CHECK TICKS ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/clean_all.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -e

echo "=== RESET COMPLET PIPELINE O-F-C-R + BUDGET ==="

# --- chemins des bases ---
DBDIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"

for db in opener follower closer recorder budget; do
  if [ -f "$DBDIR/$db.db" ]; then
    echo "🧹 Nettoyage $db.db"
    sqlite3 "$DBDIR/$db.db" "PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF; BEGIN;
      DELETE FROM sqlite_sequence;
      DELETE FROM ledger;
      DELETE FROM trades_open_init;
      DELETE FROM trades_follow;
      DELETE FROM positions_closed;
      DELETE FROM trades_record;
      DELETE FROM trades_recorded;
      DELETE FROM record_ack;
      COMMIT;" 2>/dev/null || true
  fi
done

# --- reset du budget ---
sqlite3 "$DBDIR/budget.db" "PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF; BEGIN;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ledger;
CREATE TABLE ledger (
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  src TEXT, instId TEXT, side TEXT,
  type TEXT, amount REAL,
  ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
);
INSERT INTO ledger (src, instId, side, type, amount)
VALUES ('system', 'INIT', '', 'deposit', 1000.0);
COMMIT;"

# --- re-création des vues budget ---
sqlite3 "$DBDIR/budget.db" "
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_balance;
CREATE VIEW v_balance AS
SELECT ROUND(SUM(CASE
  WHEN type IN ('deposit','pnl_real') THEN amount
  WHEN type='withdraw' THEN -amount
  ELSE 0 END),6) AS balance_usdt
FROM ledger;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_budget_overview;
CREATE VIEW v_budget_overview AS
SELECT
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='deposit' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS total_deposit,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='margin' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS total_margin,
  ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='pnl_real' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS total_pnl,
  datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM ledger;
"

echo "✅ Bases nettoyées et budget réinitialisé à 1000 USDT"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/clean_b_instid.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
TMP="/tmp/b_clean_tmp_$$.db"

echo "=== CLEAN B.DB INSTID START ==="
echo "Source: $DB"

# Copie propre
cp "$DB" "$TMP"

sqlite3 "$TMP" <<'SQL'
-- Supprime les doublons avec slash
DELETE FROM feat_1m WHERE instr(instId,'/')>0;

-- Normalise les éventuelles variantes résiduelles
UPDATE feat_1m SET instId = REPLACE(instId,'/','');

-- Vérifie le résultat
CREATE TEMP VIEW v_check AS
SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS clean, COUNT(*) AS n
FROM feat_1m GROUP BY clean ORDER BY n DESC;

SELECT 'Remaining duplicates:' AS info;
SELECT * FROM v_check WHERE n>1;
SQL

# Remplace la base propre
mv "$TMP" "$DB"
echo "=== CLEAN COMPLETED ==="
sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS rows_after_clean FROM feat_1m;"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/cleanup_ob_limited.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

MAX1=450
MAX3=150
MAX5=150

echo "===== CLEANUP OB DB (LIMITED) ====="

echo "[1] Vérification présence WAL"
rm -f "${DB}-wal" || true
rm -f "${DB}-shm" || true

echo "[2] Instruments trouvés :"
INST=$(sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM ohlcv_1m;")
echo "$INST"

cleanup_tf() {
    local TABLE=$1
    local LIMIT=$2
    local INSTID=$3

    sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
DELETE FROM ${TABLE}
WHERE instId='${INSTID}'
  AND rowid NOT IN (
    SELECT rowid FROM ${TABLE}
    WHERE instId='${INSTID}'
    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT ${LIMIT}
  );
SQL
}

echo "[3] Nettoyage coin par coin"

for I in $INST; do
    echo "   → $I (1m)"
    cleanup_tf "ohlcv_1m" $MAX1 "$I"

    if sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='ohlcv_3m';" | grep -q ohlcv_3m; then
        echo "   → $I (3m)"
        cleanup_tf "ohlcv_3m" $MAX3 "$I"
    fi

    if sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='ohlcv_5m';" | grep -q ohlcv_5m; then
        echo "   → $I (5m)"
        cleanup_tf "ohlcv_5m" $MAX5 "$I"
    fi
done

echo "[4] VACUUM (réduction réelle)"
sqlite3 "$DB" "VACUUM;"

echo "===== CLEANUP TERMINÉ ====="


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/cleanup_ohlcv.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] CLEANUP OHLCV START"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;

-- purge générique : garde les N dernières bougies par instrument
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m
WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM (
    SELECT ts, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_1m
  ) WHERE rn <= 450
);

DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m
WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM (
    SELECT ts, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_3m
  ) WHERE rn <= 150
);

DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM (
    SELECT ts, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts DESC) AS rn
    FROM ohlcv_5m
  ) WHERE rn <= 150
);

VACUUM;
SQL

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] CLEANUP OHLCV DONE"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/dash.log"
now_s=$(date +%s)
ts_now="$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
printf "\n===== SCALP PIPE HEALTH %s =====\n" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S')" | tee -a "$LOG"

check_db() {
    local name="$1" file="$2" table="$3" ts_col="$4"
    if [[ ! -f "$file" ]]; then
        printf "%-10s ❌ no DB found\n" "$name" | tee -a "$LOG"
        return
    fi
    local count ts_last age_s h m s age_hms status
    count=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    ts_last=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT MAX($ts_col)/1000 FROM $table;")
    [[ -z "$ts_last" || "$ts_last" == "0" ]] && ts_last=$now_s
    age_s=$(( now_s - ${ts_last%.*:-0} ))
    h=$((age_s/3600)); m=$(( (age_s%3600)/60 )); s=$((age_s%60))
    age_hms=$(printf "%02dh%02dm%02ds" "$h" "$m" "$s")

    if (( age_s < 10 )); then status="✅"
    elif (( age_s < 60 )); then status="⚠️"
    else status="❌"
    fi

    printf "%-10s %s  %4s recs | last=%s | age=%s\n" \
        "$name" "$status" "$count" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S' -d @$ts_last 2>/dev/null || date -r "$ts_last" '+%H:%M:%S')" "$age_hms" \
        | tee -a "$LOG"
}

check_db "opener"   "$DATA/opener.db"   "trades_open_init" "ts_create"
check_db "follower" "$DATA/follower.db" "trades_follow"    "ts_update"
check_db "closer"   "$DATA/closer.db"   "trades_close"     "ts_close"
check_db "recorder" "$DATA/recorder.db" "trades_record"    "ts_record"

printf "==============================================\n" | tee -a "$LOG"
echo "" >> "$LOG"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/diag_step_by_step.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_step.log"
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
SCRIPTS="/opt/scalp/project/scripts"
BIN="/opt/scalp/project/bin"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"

stamp(){ printf "[%s] %s\n" "$(date '+%F %T')" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }
run(){   printf "\n$ %s\n" "$*"       | tee -a "$LOG"; eval "$*"           | tee -a "$LOG"; }

stamp "=== STEP 0: ENV ==="
run "python3 -V"
run "sqlite3 -version"
run "ls -lh $DATA"
run "ls -lh $SCRIPTS"

stamp "=== STEP 1: SCHEMA REFRESH ==="
if [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/gen_schema_ref.sh" ]]; then
  run "bash $SCRIPTS/gen_schema_ref.sh"
else
  stamp "gen_schema_ref.sh absent → SKIP"
fi
test -s "$DATA/schema_ref.sql" || { stamp "schema_ref.sql manquant"; exit 1; }

stamp "=== STEP 2: SCHEMA CHECK (colonnes) ==="
if [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/diag_schema.py" ]]; then
  run "python3 $SCRIPTS/diag_schema.py"
elif [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/check_schema_all.py" ]]; then
  run "python3 $SCRIPTS/check_schema_all.py"
else
  stamp "diag_schema.py / check_schema_all.py absents → SKIP"
fi

stamp "=== STEP 3: INTEGRITY CHECK SQLite ==="
for db in "$DATA"/*.db; do
  [[ -s "$db" ]] || continue
  stamp "PRAGMA integrity_check → $(basename "$db")"
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$db\" \"PRAGMA integrity_check;\""
done

stamp "=== STEP 4: COMPILATION PYTHON ==="
find "$SCRIPTS" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name "*.py" | sort | while read -r f; do
  stamp "py_compile: $(basename "$f")"
  run "python3 -m py_compile \"$f\""
done

stamp "=== STEP 5: PIPELINE QUICK VIEWS (colonnes 100% existantes) ==="
# [O] trades_open_init (schéma_ref: instId, side, entry, sl, tp, ts_open, status, reason, score, confidence, ctx, ts_create)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/opener.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_open_init; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/opener.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,sl,tp,status,datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open FROM trades_open_init ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [F] follow_snapshot (schéma_ref: trade_uid,instId,side,entry,price,pnl_float,sl,tp,ts_update,reason_close,trigger_BE,trigger_SLtrail,trigger_PYRAMID,trigger_TIMEOUT)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/follower.db" \".tables\" | grep -qw follow_snapshot; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/follower.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,price,pnl_float,sl,tp,datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_update FROM follow_snapshot ORDER BY ts_update DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [C] trades_closed (schéma_ref: id,instId,side,pnl_real,ts_close,ts_open_ref)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/closer.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_closed; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/closer.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,pnl_real,datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close FROM trades_closed ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [R] trades_recorded (schéma_ref: trade_uid,instId,side,entry,exit,pnl_real,reason_exit,ts_open,ts_close,ctx,score_B,score_A,score_U,recorded_at)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/recorder.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_recorded; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/recorder.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,exit,pnl_real,reason_exit,datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close FROM trades_recorded ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

stamp "=== STEP 6: SCRIPTS BIN ==="
[[ -x "$BIN/check_pipeline_full.sh"     ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_pipeline_full.sh"     || stamp "check_pipeline_full.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_pipeline_timing.sh"   ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_pipeline_timing.sh"   || stamp "check_pipeline_timing.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_post_opener.sh"       ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_post_opener.sh"       || stamp "check_post_opener.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_signals_integrity.sh" ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_signals_integrity.sh" || stamp "check_signals_integrity.sh SKIP"

stamp "=== STEP 7: SELF-TESTS (--self-test si dispo) ==="
for f in "$SCRIPTS"/*.py; do
  grep -q -- "--self-test" "$f" || continue
  stamp "SELF-TEST: $(basename "$f")"
  run "python3 \"$f\" --self-test"
done

stamp "=== DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/fix_bus_out.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DATA_DIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"
shopt -s nullglob
DBS=("$DATA_DIR"/*.db)

echo "[fix_bus_out] Bases détectées:"
printf ' - %s\n' "${DBS[@]}"

for db in "${DBS[@]}"; do
  echo "[fix_bus_out] === $db ==="
  # Si la table bus_out n'existe pas, on la crée directement au bon format
  if ! sqlite3 "$db" "SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='bus_out';" | grep -q 1; then
    echo "[fix_bus_out] bus_out absente → création"
    sqlite3 "$db" "
      PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus_out(
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        src TEXT,
        instId TEXT,
        event TEXT,
        payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}',
        ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
        ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
      );
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ts  ON bus_out(ts);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack);
    "
    continue
  fi

  # Table existe → ajout conditionnel des colonnes manquantes
  has_col() { sqlite3 "$db" "PRAGMA table_info(bus_out);" | awk -F'|' '{print $2}' | grep -qx "$1"; }

  if ! has_col src;     then echo "[fix_bus_out] + colonne src";     sqlite3 "$db" "ALTER TABLE bus_out ADD COLUMN src TEXT;"; fi
  if ! has_col payload; then echo "[fix_bus_out] + colonne payload"; sqlite3 "$db" "ALTER TABLE bus_out ADD COLUMN payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}';"; fi
  if ! has_col ack;     then echo "[fix_bus_out] + colonne ack";     sqlite3 "$db" "ALTER TABLE bus_out ADD COLUMN ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0;"; fi

  # Index
  sqlite3 "$db" "
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ts  ON bus_out(ts);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack);
  "

  # Normalisation des valeurs nulles
  sqlite3 "$db" "
    UPDATE bus_out SET payload='{}' WHERE payload IS NULL;
    UPDATE bus_out SET ack=0 WHERE ack IS NULL;
  "

  # Cas particulier b.db : rétro-remplir les NEW_SIGNAL sans src/payload
  if [[ "\$db" == "$DATA_DIR/b.db" ]]; then
    echo "[fix_bus_out] b.db → backfill src/payload sur NEW_SIGNAL vides"
    sqlite3 "$db" "
      UPDATE bus_out
      SET src='signal'
      WHERE (src IS NULL OR src='')
        AND event LIKE 'NEW_SIGNAL';

      UPDATE bus_out
      SET payload=json_object(
        'side', 'buy',
        'reason', COALESCE(json_extract(payload,'$.reason'),'AUTO'),
        'score', COALESCE(json_extract(payload,'$.score'), 0),
        'confidence', COALESCE(json_extract(payload,'$.confidence'), 0.5),
        'ctx', COALESCE(json_extract(payload,'$.ctx'), 'range')
      )
      WHERE (payload IS NULL OR payload='') AND event LIKE 'NEW_SIGNAL';
    "
  fi

  echo "[fix_bus_out] OK"
done

echo "[fix_bus_out] Migration terminée."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/fix_gest_schema.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades_all (
  trade_uid   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  instId      TEXT NOT NULL,
  side        TEXT NOT NULL,
  reason      TEXT,
  ctx         TEXT,
  score_B     REAL,
  atr         REAL,
  price       REAL,
  ts_signal   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  state       TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'NEW',
  ts_open     INTEGER,
  ts_close    INTEGER,
  pnl_real    REAL DEFAULT 0,
  reason_exit TEXT
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_trades_state ON trades_all(state);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_trades_inst  ON trades_all(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_trades_ts    ON trades_all(ts_signal);

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_opener;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_follower;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_closer;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_recorder;

CREATE VIEW v_for_opener   AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='NEW';
CREATE VIEW v_for_follower AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state IN ('OPENING','ACTIVE');
CREATE VIEW v_for_closer   AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='CLOSING';
CREATE VIEW v_for_recorder AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='CLOSED';
SQL
echo "[OK] gest.db vérifié."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/fix_pipeline_full.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DBD=/opt/scalp/project/data

echo "=== FIX SCALP PIPELINE FULL ALIGNMENT ==="

# -------------------
# B : signals
# -------------------
sqlite3 "$DBD/b.db" <<'SQL'
-- vue lue par x_open
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_signals_for_open;
CREATE VIEW v_signals_for_open AS
SELECT
  id,
  instId,
  side,
  reason AS trigger,
  ctx,
  price,
  atr,
  score_U,
  score_A,
  score_B,
  ts_create AS ts,
  datetime(ts_create/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
  status
FROM signals_for_open
WHERE status='pending'
/* v_signals_for_open(id,instId,side,trigger,ctx,price,atr,score_U,score_A,score_B,ts,ts_local,status) */;
SQL

# -------------------
# O : opener
# -------------------
sqlite3 "$DBD/opener.db" <<'SQL'
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades_open_init(
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    sl REAL,
    tp REAL,
    atr REAL,
    entry_reason TEXT,
    ctx TEXT,
    score_B REAL,
    ts_create INTEGER,
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
    ts_open INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_open_inst ON trades_open_init(instId);

-- compatibilité : table attendue par x_open
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS positions_open;
CREATE VIEW positions_open AS
SELECT
    id,
    instId,
    side,
    entry,
    qty,
    sl,
    tp,
    atr,
    entry_reason,
    ctx,
    score_B,
    ts_create,
    ts_open,
    status
FROM trades_open_init;

-- vue pour follower
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_follower;
CREATE VIEW v_for_follower AS
SELECT
  instId, side, entry, sl, tp, atr, ctx, score_B, entry_reason, ts_open
FROM trades_open_init
WHERE status='pending';
SQL

# -------------------
# F : follower
# -------------------
sqlite3 "$DBD/follower.db" <<'SQL'
ALTER TABLE trades_follow ADD COLUMN ts_open INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE trades_follow ADD COLUMN ts_update INTEGER;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_close;
CREATE VIEW v_for_close AS
SELECT
  instId, side, entry, sl, tp, atr AS atr_current, ts_update AS ts_follow
FROM trades_follow
WHERE status='to_close';
SQL

# -------------------
# C : closer
# -------------------
sqlite3 "$DBD/closer.db" <<'SQL'
ALTER TABLE positions_closed ADD COLUMN ts_open INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE positions_closed ADD COLUMN atr REAL;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_recorder;
CREATE VIEW v_for_recorder AS
SELECT
  instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason_exit, atr, ts_close, ts_open
FROM positions_closed;
SQL

# -------------------
# R : recorder
# -------------------
sqlite3 "$DBD/recorder.db" <<'SQL'
ALTER TABLE trades_record ADD COLUMN ts_open INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE trades_record ADD COLUMN ts_close INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE trades_record ADD COLUMN ts_record INTEGER;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_pipeline_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_pipeline_latest AS
SELECT
  r.instId,
  r.side,
  r.entry,
  r.exit,
  r.pnl,
  r.reason_exit AS record_reason,
  r.ts_open,
  r.ts_close,
  r.ts_record,
  (r.ts_close - r.ts_open) AS trade_ms,
  (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - r.ts_close) AS age_since_close_ms
FROM trades_record r
ORDER BY r.ts_close DESC;
SQL

echo "✓ ALL MODULES ALIGNED AND COMPATIBLE"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/fix_pipeline_ofcr.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "=== SCALP - FIX PIPELINE O→F→C→R (final stable v2) ==="

DBD=/opt/scalp/project/data

add_col_safe() {
  local db="$1" table="$2" col="$3" type="$4"
  if ! sqlite3 "$db" "PRAGMA table_info($table);" | awk -F'|' '{print $2}' | grep -qx "$col"; then
    sqlite3 "$db" "ALTER TABLE $table ADD COLUMN $col $type;"
    echo "[$(basename "$db")] +$col"
  fi
}

# --- OPENER ---
add_col_safe "$DBD/opener.db" trades_open_init ts_open INTEGER
sqlite3 "$DBD/opener.db" "UPDATE trades_open_init SET ts_open=ts_create WHERE ts_open IS NULL;"
sqlite3 "$DBD/opener.db" <<'SQL'
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_open_inst ON trades_open_init(instId);
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_follower;
CREATE VIEW v_for_follower AS
SELECT instId,side,entry,sl,tp,atr,ctx,score_B,entry_reason,ts_open
FROM trades_open_init
WHERE status='pending';
SQL

# --- FOLLOWER ---
add_col_safe "$DBD/follower.db" trades_follow ts_open INTEGER
add_col_safe "$DBD/follower.db" trades_follow ts_update INTEGER
sqlite3 "$DBD/follower.db" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_close;
CREATE VIEW v_for_close AS
SELECT instId,side,entry,sl,tp,atr AS atr_current,ts_update AS ts_follow
FROM trades_follow
WHERE status='to_close';
SQL

# --- CLOSER ---
add_col_safe "$DBD/closer.db" positions_closed ts_open INTEGER
add_col_safe "$DBD/closer.db" positions_closed atr REAL

sqlite3 "$DBD/closer.db" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '${DBD}/follower.db' AS F;

UPDATE positions_closed
SET ts_open = (
  SELECT f.ts_open
  FROM F.trades_follow AS f
  WHERE f.instId = positions_closed.instId
  ORDER BY f.ts_update DESC
  LIMIT 1
)
WHERE ts_open IS NULL;

DETACH DATABASE F;
SQL

sqlite3 "$DBD/closer.db" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_recorder;
CREATE VIEW v_for_recorder AS
SELECT instId,side,entry,exit,pnl,reason_exit,atr,ts_close,ts_open
FROM positions_closed;
SQL

# --- RECORDER ---
add_col_safe "$DBD/recorder.db" trades_record ts_open INTEGER
add_col_safe "$DBD/recorder.db" trades_record ts_close INTEGER
add_col_safe "$DBD/recorder.db" trades_record ts_record INTEGER

sqlite3 "$DBD/recorder.db" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_pipeline_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_pipeline_latest AS
SELECT
  r.instId,
  r.side,
  r.entry,
  r.exit,
  r.pnl,
  r.reason_exit AS record_reason,
  r.ts_open,
  r.ts_close,
  r.ts_record,
  (r.ts_close - r.ts_open) AS trade_ms,
  (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - r.ts_close) AS age_since_close_ms
FROM trades_record r
ORDER BY r.ts_close DESC;
SQL

echo
echo "=== PIPELINE STRUCTURE VERIFIED ==="
for db in opener follower closer recorder; do
  echo "--- $db ---"
  sqlite3 "$DBD/${db}.db" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='view';"
done

echo "✓ Pipeline OFCR figée et cohérente"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/kill_ob_all.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "🧹 Nettoyage complet des collecteurs OB et des builders en double..."

# Stop service
systemctl stop scalp-ob-ws.service || true
sleep 1

# Kill all OB collectors + builders
pkill -f OB_ws_collect_v2.py || true
pkill -f OB_ws_collect.py || true
pkill -f ob_ws_singleton.sh || true
pkill -f B_feat_builder_all.py || true

echo "🔍 Process restants liés à OB ou feat:"
ps -ef | grep -E "OB_|ob_ws|feat" | grep -v grep || true

echo "🔒 Suppression lock:"
rm -f /var/lock/ob_ws.lock 2>/dev/null || true

if lsof /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "⚠️ ob.db encore utilisée:"
  lsof /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db || true
else
  echo "✅ ob.db libre."
fi

echo "✅ Tous les doublons OB_ws & builders ont été tués."

DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_1m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 450
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_3m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
VACUUM;
SQL

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] CLEAN OK" >>"$LOG"

# --- Ré-agrégation 3m ---
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || echo "agg_3m fail" >>"$LOG"

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] DONE maintenance" >>"$LOG"

fi

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_aggregate_3m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOCK="/var/lock/ob_agg3m.lock"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_agg3m.log"

exec /usr/bin/flock -n "$LOCK" bash -c "
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Start aggregation\" >> \$LOG
  sqlite3 \$DB '
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;
    INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m (instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
    SELECT instId,
           (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts_group,
           first_value(o) OVER w AS o,
           MAX(h) OVER w AS h,
           MIN(l) OVER w AS l,
           last_value(c) OVER w AS c,
           SUM(v) OVER w AS v
    FROM ohlcv_1m
    WINDOW w AS (PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000) ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 2 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)
    GROUP BY instId, ts_group;
  '
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Done\" >> \$LOG
"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_check.sh -----

.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId,
       COUNT(*) AS n,
       datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts
FROM ohlcv_1m
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY last_ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m;
VACUUM;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_kill_all.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "=== KILL OB COLLECTOR + BUILDERS ==="

echo "[1] Stop systemd..."
systemctl stop scalp-ob-ws.service 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[2] Remove lock..."
rm -f /var/lock/ob_ws.lock 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[3] Kill all python processes related to OB_ws + builder..."
pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect_v2.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f ob_ws_singleton.sh 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f B_feat_builder_all.py 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[4] Double-kill (in case of forks)..."
for i in {1..5}; do
    pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect_v2.py 2>/dev/null || true
    pkill -9 -f B_feat_builder_all.py 2>/dev/null || true
    sleep 0.2
done

echo "[5] Check remaining PIDs..."
pgrep -fl "OB_ws_collect|feat_builder|ob_ws" || echo "[OK] Aucun processus résiduel"

echo "[6] Check FD on ob.db..."
lsof /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db || echo "[OK] Aucun handle FD ouvert"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/pipeline_diagnostics.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_O="/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_F="/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_C="/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

sqlite3 "$DB_C" <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_O"' AS O;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_F"' AS F;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_B"' AS B;
.headers on
.mode column

WITH sig AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_signal_s
  FROM B.signals_B
  GROUP BY instId
),
open AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts_open) AS ts_open
  FROM O.trades_open_init
  GROUP BY instId
),
closed AS (
  SELECT instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason_exit, atr, ts_open, ts_close
  FROM main.positions_closed
)
SELECT
  c.instId,
  c.side,
  c.reason_exit,
  printf('%.4f', c.pnl) AS pnl,
  (c.ts_close - c.ts_open) AS trade_ms,
  CASE WHEN s.ts_signal_s IS NULL THEN NULL
       ELSE (c.ts_open - s.ts_signal_s*1000)
  END AS open_latency_ms
FROM closed c
LEFT JOIN sig s   ON s.instId = c.instId
LEFT JOIN open o  ON o.instId = c.instId AND o.ts_open = c.ts_open
ORDER BY c.ts_close DESC
LIMIT 50;

DETACH DATABASE O;
DETACH DATABASE F;
DETACH DATABASE B;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/rebuild_signals_for_open.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

echo "[SYNC] Import fresh ctx into b.db as ctx_cache"
sqlite3 "$DB_B" <<SQL
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ctx_cache;
CREATE TABLE ctx_cache AS
SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, ctx, ts
FROM '${DB_A}'.ctx_a_latest;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ctx_cache_instId ON ctx_cache(instId);
SQL

echo "[REBUILD] signals_for_open using ctx_cache"
sqlite3 "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS signals_for_open;
CREATE VIEW signals_for_open AS
SELECT
    b.id,
    b.instId,
    b.side,
    b.reason,
    COALESCE(c.ctx, 'unknown') AS ctx,
    b.price,
    b.atr,
    b.score_U,
    b.score_A,
    b.score_B,
    b.ts_signal,
    datetime(b.ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
    'pending' AS status
FROM signals_B b
LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c
  ON REPLACE(b.instId,'/','') = c.instId
WHERE b.ts_signal IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY b.ts_signal DESC;
SQL

echo "[OK] signals_for_open rebuilt successfully with ctx_cache"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/relaunch_ohlcv_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== RELANCE OHLCV + FEAT ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

# --- stop services ---
echo "[1] Stop services"
systemctl stop scalp-ob.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-oa.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.timer || true

# --- kill python leftover ---
echo "[2] Kill runaway processes"
pkill -f OB_collect.py || true
pkill -f OA_ohlcv_A.py || true
pkill -f B_feat_builder || true

# --- cleanup OHLCV if old ---
DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
echo "[3] Check OHLCV timestamps"

AGE1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)
AGE5=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_5m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( AGE1 > 300 || AGE5 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ OHLCV trop vieux → reset tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m;"
else
    echo "OK OHLCV pas trop vieux"
fi

# --- cleanup feat if old ---
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
echo "[4] Check FEAT timestamps"

F1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM feat_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( F1 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ Features trop vieux → reset feat tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_5m;"
fi

# --- restart pipeline ---
echo "[5] Restart OA"
systemctl start scalp-oa.service

echo "[6] Restart OB"
systemctl start scalp-ob.service

echo "[7] Restart feat builder (timer)"
systemctl start scalp-b-feat-builder.timer

echo "===== RELANCE OK ====="

echo "[8] Vérification dans 10 secondes…"
sleep 10

echo "--- OHLCV FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'

echo "--- FEAT FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_feat_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/reset_all.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -e

echo "=== 🔄 RESET PIPELINE COMPLET ==="

# 1️⃣ Stopper tous les services SCALP
systemctl stop scalp-opener.service 2>/dev/null || true
systemctl stop scalp-follower.service 2>/dev/null || true
systemctl stop scalp-closer.service 2>/dev/null || true
systemctl stop scalp-recorder.service 2>/dev/null || true

# 2️⃣ Nettoyer les tables
for db in /opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db /opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db /opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db /opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db; do
  if [ -f "$db" ]; then
    echo "Nettoyage $db"
    sqlite3 "$db" "DELETE FROM sqlite_sequence;"
    sqlite3 "$db" "DELETE FROM trades_open_init;" 2>/dev/null || true
    sqlite3 "$db" "DELETE FROM trades_follow;" 2>/dev/null || true
    sqlite3 "$db" "DELETE FROM positions_closed;" 2>/dev/null || true
  fi
done

# 3️⃣ Réinitialiser le budget
sqlite3 /opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db <<'SQL'
UPDATE budget_state
SET balance=1000.0, margin=0.0, pnl_real=0.0,
    ts_update=strftime('%s','now');
DELETE FROM ledger;
SQL

echo "Budget réinitialisé à 1000 USDT"

# 4️⃣ Vérification
sqlite3 -header -column /opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db "SELECT * FROM budget_state;"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/reset_gest_data.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_DIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"

echo "[RESET] purge des données tout en gardant la structure…"

for db in gest opener follower closer recorder; do
  FILE="${DB_DIR}/${db}.db"
  if [ -f "$FILE" ]; then
    echo "→ nettoyage $db.db"
    sqlite3 "$FILE" <<'SQL'
      DELETE FROM trades;
      DELETE FROM trades_all;
      DELETE FROM signals_in;
      DELETE FROM open_snapshot;
      DELETE FROM follow_snapshot;
      DELETE FROM close_snapshot;
      DELETE FROM record_snapshot;
      UPDATE budget_state SET balance=1000,equity=1000,margin=0,ts_update=strftime('%s','now')*1000 WHERE id=1;
      VACUUM;
SQL
  fi
done

echo "[RESET] terminé — bases vides, schéma intact."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/reset_ofcr.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
DBS=(opener follower closer recorder)
echo "===== RESET O-F-C-R DATABASES (SAFE) ====="

for db in "${DBS[@]}"; do
  FILE="${DATA}/${db}.db"
  [[ -f "$FILE" ]] || continue
  echo "-- $db.db"
  tables=$(sqlite3 "$FILE" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';")
  for t in $tables; do
    sqlite3 "$FILE" "DELETE FROM $t;" || true
  done
  sqlite3 "$FILE" "VACUUM;"
done

echo "Killing Python instances..."
pkill -f opener.py || true
pkill -f follower.py || true
pkill -f closer.py || true
pkill -f recorder.py || true

echo "Restarting services..."
systemctl restart scalp-opener.service
systemctl restart scalp-follower.service
systemctl restart scalp-closer.service
systemctl restart scalp-recorder.service

echo "===== RESET COMPLETE ====="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/reset_ofr.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"

echo "===== RESET FOLLOWER / CLOSER / RECORDER ====="

for db in follower closer recorder; do
  FILE="${DATA}/${db}.db"
  if [ -f "$FILE" ]; then
    echo "-- purge ${db}.db"
    sqlite3 "$FILE" "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;"
    tables=$(sqlite3 "$FILE" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name NOT LIKE 'sqlite_%';")
    for t in $tables; do
      sqlite3 "$FILE" "DELETE FROM $t;" || true
    done
    sqlite3 "$FILE" "VACUUM;"
  fi
done

echo
echo "Killing running instances..."
pkill -f follower.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f closer.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f recorder.py 2>/dev/null || true

echo "✅ Databases purged & processes stopped"
echo "You can now restart follower normally."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/reset_x_pipeline.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "=== RESET X PIPELINE ==="

DB_DIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"

stop_service() {
  systemctl stop "$1" 2>/dev/null || true
}

# --- 1. Stop services
for svc in scalp-opener scalp-follower scalp-closer scalp-recorder; do
  stop_service "$svc.service"
done
sleep 1

# --- 2. Cleanup with table existence checks
for db in opener.db follower.db closer.db recorder.db; do
  path="${DB_DIR}/${db}"
  [ ! -f "$path" ] && continue
  echo "→ cleaning $db"

  tables=$(sqlite3 "$path" ".tables")
  [[ -z "$tables" ]] && continue

  for table in $tables; do
    sqlite3 "$path" "DELETE FROM $table;" 2>/dev/null || true
  done

  sqlite3 "$path" "DELETE FROM sqlite_sequence;" 2>/dev/null || true
done

# --- 3. Vacuum cleanup
for db in opener.db follower.db closer.db recorder.db; do
  path="${DB_DIR}/${db}"
  [ -f "$path" ] && sqlite3 "$path" "VACUUM;" 2>/dev/null || true
done

echo "=== RESET DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/safe_agg_3m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
echo "=== SAFE 3M AGG $(date '+%F %T') ==="
# Attente si DB utilisée
for i in {1..30}; do
  if lsof "$DB" | grep -q python3; then
    echo "⏳ Attente libération ob.db ($i/30)"
    sleep 2
  else
    bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh
    exit 0
  fi
done
echo "❌ Timeout : ob.db toujours utilisée."
exit 1

if [ "$sec" != "00" ]; then
  wait=$((60 - sec))
  echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] attente ${wait}s pour top-minute..." | tee -a "$LOG"
  sleep $wait
fi

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] lancement OB_collect.py (1m)" | tee -a "$LOG"

-- Mise à jour de feat_1m.ctx avec le contexte réel de A
UPDATE feat_1m
SET ctx = (
    SELECT ctx_a.ctx
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
)
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
);

DETACH DATABASE A;

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"
SERVICES=(
  scalp-signal.service
  scalp-opener.service
  scalp-follower.service
  scalp-closer.service
  scalp-recorder.service
  scalp-budget.service
  scalp-gest-bus.service
)

clear
echo "===== SCALP SYSTEM HEALTH DASH ====="
echo "📅 $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
echo

# ---- 1. SYSTEMD STATUS ----
printf "%-22s %-8s %-10s\n" "SERVICE" "STATUS" "PID"
echo "---------------------------------------------"

for svc in "${SERVICES[@]}"; do
  if systemctl is-active --quiet "$svc"; then
    pid=$(systemctl show -p MainPID --value "$svc")
    printf "%-22s ✅ %-8s %-10s\n" "$svc" "active" "$pid"
  else
    printf "%-22s ❌ %-8s\n" "$svc" "inactive"
  fi
done

echo
echo "---- 2. BUS EVENTS ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 8 8 22
SELECT src AS MODULE,
       COUNT(*) AS TOTAL,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-300)*1000) AS LAST5MIN,
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS LAST_EVENT
FROM bus_events
GROUP BY src
ORDER BY src;
SQL

echo
echo "---- 3. LATEST 10 EVENTS ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<'SQL'
.headers off
.mode column
.width 10 14 14 22
SELECT src, instId, event, datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM bus_events
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

echo
echo "---- 4. SUMMARY ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" "SELECT COUNT(*) AS total_events, COUNT(DISTINCT src) AS modules, MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_event FROM bus_events;"

echo
echo "✅ DASH refresh every 10s (Ctrl+C to quit)"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/follower_pnl_float.sql -----
-- ===========================================
-- Vue : v_pnl_float
-- But : afficher le PnL flottant (non réalisé)
--       pour chaque position active ou ouverte
-- ===========================================

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_pnl_float;

CREATE VIEW v_pnl_float AS
SELECT
    f.instId,
    f.side,
    f.entry,
    t.lastPr AS last,
    ROUND(
        CASE
            WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.lastPr - f.entry) * f.qty * f.leverage
            WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.lastPr) * f.qty * f.leverage
            ELSE 0
        END, 6
    ) AS pnl_float_usdt,
    ROUND(f.qty * f.entry * f.leverage, 6) AS notional_usdt,
    datetime(t.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_tick
FROM trades_follow f
LEFT JOIN main.v_ticks_latest t
  ON REPLACE(t.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')
WHERE f.status IN ('active','open');

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/init_bus.sql -----
-- =========================================================
--   SCALP CENTRAL BUS  —  Communication inter-modules
-- =========================================================

PRAGMA journal_mode = WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous = NORMAL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    stage TEXT NOT NULL,          -- ex: "B→GEST", "GEST→OPEN", etc.
    source TEXT NOT NULL,         -- module émetteur
    dest TEXT NOT NULL,           -- module récepteur
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,         -- ex: BTC/USDT
    payload TEXT,                 -- JSON libre
    ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
    ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_dest_ack ON bus(dest, ack);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_stage ON bus(stage);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_inst ON bus(instId);

-- VUES DE DIAGNOSTIC
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_pending AS
SELECT stage, dest, COUNT(*) AS pending
FROM bus
WHERE ack=0
GROUP BY stage, dest;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_last_msg AS
SELECT stage, dest, instId,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
       payload
FROM bus
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 50;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_pipeline_health AS
SELECT dest,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=0) AS pending,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=1) AS processed,
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_activity
FROM bus
GROUP BY dest;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_activity_last_5min AS
SELECT stage, dest,
       COUNT(*) AS recent_msgs
FROM bus
WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-300)*1000
GROUP BY stage, dest;

);

FROM bus_events

LIMIT 50;

       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_ts
FROM bus_events

ORDER BY last_ts DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/q_follow_pnl_float.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db' AS tdb;

WITH ticks AS (
  SELECT
    instId,
    lastPr AS last,
    datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_last
  FROM tdb.v_ticks_latest
)
SELECT
  f.instId,
  f.side,
  ROUND(f.entry, 4) AS entry,
  ROUND(t.last, 4) AS last,
  ROUND(
    CASE
      WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.last - f.entry) / f.entry * 100
      WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.last) / f.entry * 100
      ELSE 0 END, 2
  ) AS pnl_pct,
  ROUND(
    CASE
      WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.last - f.entry) * f.qty * f.leverage
      WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.last) * f.qty * f.leverage
      ELSE 0 END, 2
  ) AS pnl_usdt,
  ROUND(f.tp, 4) AS tp,
  ROUND(f.sl, 4) AS sl,
  f.status,
  datetime(f.ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS opened_at,
  t.ts_last AS last_tick
FROM trades_follow f
LEFT JOIN ticks t
  ON REPLACE(f.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(t.instId,'/','')
WHERE f.status IN ('active','open','pending')
ORDER BY f.ts_open DESC;

DETACH DATABASE tdb;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/v_signals_coin_overview.sql -----
CREATE VIEW v_signals_coin_overview AS
WITH last_sig AS (
    SELECT 
        REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst_key,
        instId,
        side,
        reason AS trigger,
        score_B,
        ts_signal,
        datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
        printf('%02d:%02d:%02d',
               (strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)/3600,
               ((strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)/60)%60,
               (strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)%60) AS age_hms,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY REPLACE(instId,'/','') ORDER BY ts_signal DESC) AS rn
    FROM signals_B
)
SELECT 
    u.instId,
    COALESCE(c.ctx, 'unknown') AS ctx,
    ls.side,
    ls.trigger,
    ROUND(ls.score_B,2) AS score_B,
    ls.ts_local,
    ls.age_hms
FROM universe u
LEFT JOIN last_sig ls
  ON REPLACE(u.instId,'/','') = ls.inst_key AND ls.rn = 1
LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c
  ON REPLACE(u.instId,'/','') = c.instId
ORDER BY ls.ts_signal DESC;
