----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_analyse.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, math, time

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_U = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
TF = "5m"

def softmax(x):
    e = [math.exp(i) for i in x]
    s = sum(e)
    return [v/s for v in e]

def get_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)
    rows = con.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId").fetchall()
    con.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]

def load_ob(inst):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    row = con.execute(f"SELECT rsi FROM ob_{TF} WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1", (inst,)).fetchone()
    con.close()
    return row[0] if row else None

def compute_ctx(rsi):
    if rsi < 30: return "bullish"
    if rsi > 70: return "bearish"
    if 45 <= rsi <= 55: return "range"
    return "none"

def compute_score_A(ctx):
    if ctx == "bullish": return 0.8
    if ctx == "bearish": return -0.8
    if ctx == "range": return 0.0
    return 0.0

def run():
    insts = get_universe()
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    out = []

    for inst in insts:
        rsi = load_ob(inst)
        if rsi is None:
            continue
        ctx = compute_ctx(rsi)
        score_A = compute_score_A(ctx)
        p_buy, p_sell = softmax([score_A, -score_A])
        out.append((inst, now, 0.0, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx))

    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    con.execute("DELETE FROM ctx_a_latest")
    con.executemany("INSERT INTO ctx_a_latest(instId,ts,score_U,score_A,p_buy,p_sell,ctx) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", out)
    con.commit()
    con.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_config.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3

# DB paths
DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_OA = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"
DB_U  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

# TF used
TF_SHORT = "5m"
TF_MED   = "15m"
TF_LONG  = "30m"

# Weights for score (softmax later)
W_SHORT = 0.50
W_MED   = 0.30
W_LONG  = 0.20

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_ctx.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, numpy as np

DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_OA = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"
DB_U  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

# --- paramètres de pondération ---
W = dict(EMA=0.35, MACD=0.25, RSI=0.20, ADX=0.10, OBV=0.10)
TF_WEIGHTS = {"30m":0.5, "15m":0.3, "5m":0.2}
TAU = 0.35

# --- fonctions utilitaires ---
def ema(arr, n):
    if len(arr) < n: return None
    k = 2/(n+1)
    e = arr[0]
    for x in arr[1:]:
        e = k*x + (1-k)*e
    return e

def atr(high, low, close, period=14):
    tr = [max(h-l, abs(h-cp), abs(l-cp)) for h,l,cp in zip(high[1:],low[1:],close[:-1])]
    return np.mean(tr[-period:]) if tr else 0

def rsi(vals, period=14):
    if len(vals) < period+1: return 50
    diffs = np.diff(vals)
    up = np.mean([d for d in diffs[-period:] if d>0]) or 1e-9
    dn = np.mean([-d for d in diffs[-period:] if d<0]) or 1e-9
    rs = up/dn
    return 100 - 100/(1+rs)

def adx(high, low, close, period=14):
    if len(high) < period+2: return 20
    plus_dm = np.maximum(np.diff(high), 0)
    minus_dm = np.maximum(-np.diff(low), 0)
    tr = np.maximum(high[1:]-low[1:], np.abs(high[1:]-close[:-1]))
    tr = np.maximum(tr, np.abs(low[1:]-close[:-1]))
    tr_sm = np.mean(tr[-period:])
    plus = 100*np.mean(plus_dm[-period:])/tr_sm if tr_sm else 0
    minus = 100*np.mean(minus_dm[-period:])/tr_sm if tr_sm else 0
    dx = abs(plus - minus)/(plus + minus + 1e-9)*100
    return dx

def macd(vals):
    e12, e26 = ema(vals,12), ema(vals,26)
    if e12 is None or e26 is None: return 0
    hist = e12 - e26
    return hist

def softmax3(s, tau=TAU):
    exp_pos = np.exp(s/tau)
    exp_neg = np.exp(-s/tau)
    denom = exp_pos + 1 + exp_neg
    return exp_pos/denom, exp_neg/denom, 1 - (exp_pos+exp_neg)/denom

# --- extraction OHLCV ---
def fetch_tf(con, inst, tf):
    q = f"SELECT ts, open, high, low, close, volume FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150"
    rows = con.execute(q, (inst,)).fetchall()
    if not rows: return None
    arr = np.array(rows[::-1])
    return arr[:,1], arr[:,2], arr[:,3], arr[:,4], arr[:,5]

# --- score par timeframe ---
def score_tf(o,h,l,c,v):
    c = c.astype(float)
    atrv = atr(h,l,c)
    s_ema  = np.tanh((ema(c,12) - ema(c,26)) / (max(atrv,1e-8)))
    s_macd = np.tanh(macd(c) / (np.std(c) + 1e-8))
    s_rsi  = (rsi(c)-50)/50
    s_adx  = np.clip((adx(h,l,c)-20)/20, -1, 1)
    s_obv  = np.tanh(np.diff(v)[-1] / (np.median(np.abs(v[-20:])) + 1e-8))
    return np.average([s_ema,s_macd,s_rsi,s_adx,s_obv], weights=list(W.values()))

# --- score multi-TF ---
def score_multi(tf_scores):
    vals = [tf_scores.get(tf,0)*TF_WEIGHTS[tf] for tf in TF_WEIGHTS]
    return sum(vals)

def main():
    ts_now = int(time.time()*1000)
    con_a = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    con_oa = sqlite3.connect(DB_OA)
    con_u = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)

    insts = [r[0] for r in con_u.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe")]

    rows_out=[]
    for inst in insts:
        tf_scores={}
        for tf in TF_WEIGHTS.keys():
            data = fetch_tf(con_oa, inst, tf)
            if data is None: continue
            o,h,l,c,v = data
            tf_scores[tf] = score_tf(o,h,l,c,v)
        if not tf_scores: continue
        s = score_multi(tf_scores)

        p_buy,p_sell,p_hold = softmax3(s)
        if p_buy>=0.6: ctx="bullish"
        elif p_sell>=0.6: ctx="bearish"
        else: ctx="range"

        score_U = 0.0
        score_A = abs(s)
        rows_out.append((inst, ts_now, score_U, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx))

    cur = con_a.cursor()
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM ctx_a_latest")
    cur.executemany("""
        INSERT INTO ctx_a_latest(instId,ts,score_U,score_A,p_buy,p_sell,ctx)
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    """, rows_out)
    con_a.commit()
    con_a.close(); con_oa.close(); con_u.close()
    print(f"[A] ✓ ctx_A updated (multi-indicator, {len(rows_out)} inst.)")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_ctx_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, datetime, time

DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_OA = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"

def fmt(ts_ms):
    return datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(ts_ms / 1000).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

def check_last_candles():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_OA)
    cur = con.cursor()
    now = int(time.time())
    out = []
    limits = {"5m": 300, "15m": 900, "30m": 1800}
    for tf in ("5m", "15m", "30m"):
        row = cur.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_{tf}").fetchone()
        if row and row[0]:
            ts = int(row[0] / 1000)
            age = now - ts
            limit = limits[tf]
            mark = "✅" if age < limit else "⚠️"
            out.append((tf, fmt(row[0]), f"{age}s", mark))
        else:
            out.append((tf, "N/A", "-", "❌"))
    con.close()
    return out

def summary_ctx():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    cur = con.cursor()
    rows = cur.execute("""
        SELECT ctx, GROUP_CONCAT(instId, ' ') AS coins,
               COUNT(*) AS n, MAX(ts) AS last_ts
        FROM ctx_a_latest
        GROUP BY ctx
        ORDER BY ctx
    """).fetchall()
    total = sum(r[2] for r in rows)
    print("===== CTX SUMMARY (A) =====")
    for ctx, coins, n, last_ts in rows:
        hms = datetime.datetime.fromtimestamp(last_ts / 1000).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        subset = " ".join(coins.split(" ")[:5]) if coins else ""
        print(f"{ctx:<7} | {n:<2} | {subset} | {hms}")
    print("---------------------------")
    print(f"TOTAL   | {total}")
    print("===========================")
    con.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=== LAST OA CANDLES USED ===")
    print("tf   last_candle           age     status")
    print("--   -------------------   -------  -------")
    for tf, last, age, mark in check_last_candles():
        print(f"{tf:<4} {last:<20} {age:<7} {mark}")
    print()
    summary_ctx()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# SCALP - Feature Builder (1m/3m/5m) stable
import sqlite3
import logging
import pandas as pd
import time
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
OB_DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename="/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder.log",
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s B_FEAT %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)

MAX_1M = 450
MAX_3M = 150
MAX_5M = 150

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# DB CONNECT
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def connect_db(path):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=5000, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return conn

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# LOAD OHLCV 1M
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def load_1m(inst):
    conn = connect_db(OB_DB)
    q = f"""
    SELECT ts, o, h, l, c, v
    FROM ohlcv_1m
    WHERE instId='{inst}'
    ORDER BY ts ASC;
    """
    df = pd.read_sql_query(q, conn)
    conn.close()
    return df

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# FEATURES
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def compute_features(df):
    if df.empty:
        return df

    df["ema12"] = df["c"].ewm(span=12, adjust=False).mean()
    df["ema26"] = df["c"].ewm(span=26, adjust=False).mean()
    df["rsi14"] = _rsi(df["c"], 14)
    df["atr14"] = _atr(df, 14)
    return df

def _rsi(series, n=14):
    delta = series.diff()
    gain = delta.clip(lower=0).ewm(span=n, adjust=False).mean()
    loss = (-delta.clip(upper=0)).ewm(span=n, adjust=False).mean()
    rs = gain / (loss + 1e-12)
    return 100 - 100 / (1 + rs)

def _atr(df, n=14):
    tr = (df["h"] - df["l"]).abs()
    return tr.ewm(span=n, adjust=False).mean()

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# WRITE FEATURES
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def write_feat(conn, inst, df, table):
    cur = conn.cursor()
    sql = f"""
    INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table}(instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v, ema12, ema26, rsi14, atr14)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
    """
    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        rows.append((inst, int(r.ts), float(r.o), float(r.h), float(r.l),
                     float(r.c), float(r.v),
                     float(r.ema12), float(r.ema26),
                     float(r.rsi14), float(r.atr14)))
    cur.executemany(sql, rows)
    conn.commit()

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# CLEANUP PER COIN
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def cleanup(conn, inst, table, limit):
    q = f"""
    DELETE FROM {table}
    WHERE instId='{inst}'
      AND rowid NOT IN (
        SELECT rowid FROM {table}
        WHERE instId='{inst}'
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT {limit}
      );
    """
    conn.execute(q)

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# MAIN
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    logging.info("start")

    uconn = connect_db("/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db")
    universe = [r[0].replace("/", "") for r in uconn.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe;")]
    uconn.close()

    conn = connect_db(DB)

    for inst in universe:
        df = load_1m(inst)
        if df.empty:
            continue

        df_feat = compute_features(df)
        write_feat(conn, inst, df_feat, "feat_1m")
        cleanup(conn, inst, "feat_1m", MAX_1M)

    logging.info("end")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder_all.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
SCALP - B_FEAT_BUILDER_ALL
Génération des features EMA/RSI/ATR/Bollinger pour les TF 1m,3m,5m
Sources : ob.db → Destination : b.db
Univers dynamique (u.db)
"""

import sqlite3, pandas as pd, numpy as np, time, logging
from datetime import datetime

DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_U  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOG_FILE = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder_all.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [B_FEAT_BUILDER] %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG_FILE), logging.StreamHandler()]
)
log = logging.getLogger("B_FEAT_BUILDER")

def connect(db):
    con = sqlite3.connect(db, timeout=10)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return con

def get_universe():
    con = connect(DB_U)
    df = pd.read_sql("SELECT instId FROM universe;", con)
    con.close()
    return [x.replace("/", "") for x in df["instId"].tolist()]

def ema(s, span): return s.ewm(span=span, adjust=False).mean()
def rsi(s, p=14):
    d = s.diff(); up = d.clip(lower=0).rolling(p).mean(); dn = -d.clip(upper=0).rolling(p).mean()
    rs = up / dn; return 100 - (100/(1+rs))
def atr(df, p=14):
    hl = df.h - df.l
    hc = (df.h - df.c.shift()).abs()
    lc = (df.l - df.c.shift()).abs()
    tr = pd.concat([hl, hc, lc], axis=1).max(axis=1)
    return tr.rolling(p).mean()
def boll(df, p=20):
    m = df.c.rolling(p).mean(); s = df.c.rolling(p).std()
    up, lo = m+2*s, m-2*s; w = (up-lo)/m
    return m, s, up, lo, w

def compute(df):
    if df.empty: return df
    df["ema12"]=ema(df.c,12); df["ema26"]=ema(df.c,26)
    df["rsi14"]=rsi(df.c,14); df["atr14"]=atr(df,14)
    df["bb_mid"],df["bb_std"],df["bb_up"],df["bb_low"],df["bb_width"]=boll(df,20)
    return df

def build_tf(tf):
    start=time.time(); con_src=connect(DB_OB); con_dst=connect(DB_B)
    con_dst.execute(f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_{tf} (
        ts INTEGER,o REAL,h REAL,l REAL,c REAL,v REAL,
        ema12 REAL,ema26 REAL,rsi14 REAL,atr14 REAL,
        bb_mid REAL,bb_std REAL,bb_up REAL,bb_low REAL,bb_width REAL,
        instId TEXT);"""); con_dst.commit()
    insts=get_universe(); n=0
    for inst in insts:
        try:
            q=f"SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId='{inst}' ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 500;"
            df=pd.read_sql_query(q,con_src)
            if df.empty: continue
            df=df.sort_values("ts").reset_index(drop=True)
            df=compute(df).dropna()
            if df.empty: continue
            last=df.iloc[-1:].copy(); last["instId"]=inst
            last.to_sql(f"feat_{tf}",con_dst,if_exists="append",index=False)
            n+=1
        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"{inst} {tf}: {e}")
    con_src.close(); con_dst.commit(); con_dst.close()
    log.info(f"{n} instruments mis à jour dans feat_{tf} en {time.time()-start:.2f}s")

def main():
    log.info("→ Démarrage builder (1m/3m/5m)")
    for tf in ["1m","3m","5m"]: build_tf(tf)
    log.info("✅ Terminé")

if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, sys, os

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
MAX_1M = 450
MAX_3M = 150
MAX_5M = 150

def connect_db():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5000, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return conn

def cleanup_tf(conn, table, limit):
    q = f"""
    DELETE FROM {table}
    WHERE rowid NOT IN (
        SELECT rowid FROM {table}
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT {limit}
    );
    """
    conn.execute(q)

def safe_build():
    conn = connect_db()
    cur = conn.cursor()

    try:
        cur.execute("SELECT 1;")
    except Exception as e:
        print("DB locked:", e)
        return False

    try:
        cleanup_tf(conn, "feat_1m", MAX_1M)
        cleanup_tf(conn, "feat_3m", MAX_3M)
        cleanup_tf(conn, "feat_5m", MAX_5M)
        conn.commit()
    except Exception as e:
        print("Cleanup error:", e)
        return False

    rc = os.system("python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder.py")
    return rc == 0

def main():
    ok = safe_build()
    if not ok:
        print("SAFE-BUILDER: retry in 2s…")
        time.sleep(2)
        safe_build()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_signals.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, sys, traceback
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()
        cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out(instId,event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        print(f"[SIGNAL] {instId} → {event}", flush=True)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[SIGNAL ERR][bus_notify] {e}", flush=True)

def main():
    print("[SIGNAL] Service started.", flush=True)
    while True:
        try:
            conn = get_conn()
            cur = conn.cursor()
            cur.execute("""
                SELECT id, instId, side, reason, score, ctx, ts
                FROM triggers
                WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-60)*1000
                ORDER BY ts DESC
                LIMIT 50;
            """)
            rows = cur.fetchall()
            n_signals = 0
            for r in rows:
                cur.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO signals_B(instId,side,reason,score_B,ctx,ts_signal)
                    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)
                """, (r["instId"],r["side"],r["reason"],r["score"],r["ctx"],r["ts"]))
                bus_notify(r["instId"], "NEW_SIGNAL")
                n_signals += 1
            conn.commit()
            conn.close()
            print(f"[SIGNAL] {datetime.now()} → {n_signals} signaux générés.", flush=True)
            time.sleep(10)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[SIGNAL ERR] {e}", flush=True)
            traceback.print_exc()
            time.sleep(3)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_triggers.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import sqlite3, time, logging, math

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_triggers.log"
DB_B = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_TRIGGERS] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
)

def ensure_tables(cur):
    cur.executescript("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS triggers (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        instId TEXT NOT NULL,
        side TEXT,
        reason TEXT,
        score REAL,
        confidence REAL,
        ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
    );
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_trig_inst_ts ON triggers(instId, ts DESC);

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus_out (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        src TEXT,
        instId TEXT,
        event TEXT,
        payload TEXT,
        ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
    );
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_ts ON bus_out(ts);
    """)

def fetch_features(cur):
    cur.execute("""
    SELECT instId, rsi14_1m, slope_ema12_1m, ctx, ts
    FROM feat_1m
    WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 900000
    ORDER BY ts DESC;
    """)
    return cur.fetchall()

def compute_score(rsi, slope, ctx):
    base = abs(rsi - 50)
    slope_factor = abs(slope) * 5000
    ctx_boost = 1.0
    if ctx == 'bullish' and slope > 0:
        ctx_boost = 1.2
    elif ctx == 'bearish' and slope < 0:
        ctx_boost = 1.2
    elif ctx == 'range':
        ctx_boost = 0.7
    score = min(100.0, base + slope_factor * ctx_boost)
    conf = min(1.0, score / 100.0)
    return score, conf

def detect_triggers(cur, rows):
    out = []
    for instId, rsi, slope, ctx, ts in rows:
        if rsi is None or slope is None:
            continue
        side, reason = None, None

        if rsi > 68 and slope < 0:
            side, reason = 'sell', 'RSI_OVERBOUGHT'
        elif rsi < 32 and slope > 0:
            side, reason = 'buy', 'RSI_OVERSOLD'
        elif abs(slope) > 0.015:
            side = 'buy' if slope > 0 else 'sell'
            reason = 'MOMENTUM_BREAK'
        else:
            continue

        cur.execute("""
            SELECT COUNT(*) FROM triggers
            WHERE instId=? AND side=? AND ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 120000;
        """, (instId, side))
        if cur.fetchone()[0] == 0:
            score, conf = compute_score(rsi, slope, ctx)
            out.append((instId, side, reason, round(score,2), round(conf,3), int(time.time()*1000)))
    return out

def insert_triggers(cur, triggers):
    if not triggers:
        return 0
    cur.executemany("""
        INSERT INTO triggers (instId, side, reason, score, confidence, ts)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
    """, triggers)
    cur.executemany("""
        INSERT INTO bus_out (src, instId, event, payload)
        VALUES ('signal', ?, 'NEW_TRIGGER',
                json_object('side', ?, 'reason', ?, 'score', ?, 'confidence', ?));
    """, [(t[0], t[1], t[2], t[3], t[4]) for t in triggers])
    return len(triggers)

def cleanup(cur):
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM triggers WHERE ts < strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 3600000;")
    cur.execute("""
        DELETE FROM bus_out
        WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT id FROM bus_out ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10000);
    """)

def main():
    logging.info("Démarrage.")
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    ensure_tables(cur)
    rows = fetch_features(cur)
    triggers = detect_triggers(cur, rows)
    inserted = insert_triggers(cur, triggers)
    cleanup(cur)
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    logging.info(f"{inserted} triggers insérés.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/H_perf.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, statistics, logging, sys
from pathlib import Path

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/H_perf.log"
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG), logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)]
)

DB_CLOSED = "/opt/scalp/project/data/x_closed.db"
DB_H = "/opt/scalp/project/data/h.db"

def connect_db(path):
    con = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return con

def ensure_closed_schema():
    con = connect_db(DB_CLOSED)
    con.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_closed(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            instId TEXT, side TEXT, entry REAL, exit REAL,
            sl REAL, tp REAL, pnl REAL, reason TEXT,
            ts_open INTEGER, ts_close INTEGER
        )
    """)
    con.close()

def migrate_h():
    con = connect_db(DB_H)
    con.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS score_H(
            instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            avg_pnl REAL,
            winrate REAL,
            trades INTEGER,
            last_update INTEGER
        )
    """)
    con.close()

def compute_score():
    ensure_closed_schema()
    con_c = connect_db(DB_CLOSED)
    rows = con_c.execute("SELECT instId, pnl FROM positions_closed").fetchall()
    con_c.close()
    if not rows:
        logging.info("Aucun trade clos, pas de calcul.")
        return
    data = {}
    for inst,pnl in rows:
        data.setdefault(inst,[]).append(pnl)
    con_h = connect_db(DB_H)
    for inst,vals in data.items():
        avg = statistics.mean(vals)
        winrate = sum(1 for v in vals if v>0)/len(vals)
        con_h.execute("""
            INSERT OR REPLACE INTO score_H(instId,avg_pnl,winrate,trades,last_update)
            VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)
        """,(inst,avg,winrate,len(vals),int(time.time()*1000)))
    con_h.close()
    logging.info(f"Scores H mis à jour pour {len(data)} instruments.")

def main(argv):
    migrate_h()
    compute_score()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OA_ohlcv_A.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, ccxt

DBU = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
DBO = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"
TF_LIST = ["5m","15m","30m"]
INIT = 150
MAX_ROWS = 300

ex = ccxt.bitget()

def to_bitget_symbol(inst: str) -> str:
    return inst if ":" in inst else f"{inst}:USDT"

def ensure_schema():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        cur.execute(f"DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}")
        cur.execute(f"""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}(
          instId TEXT,
          ts INTEGER,
          open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
          PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
        )
        """)
    con.commit()
    con.close()

def load_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBU, timeout=5)
    rows = [r[0] for r in con.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe")]
    con.close()
    return rows

def last_ts(con, tf, inst):
    row = con.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId=?", (inst,)).fetchone()
    return row[0] if row and row[0] is not None else None

def upsert_batch(tf, inst, batch):
    if not batch:
        return
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.executemany(
        f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ohlcv_{tf}(instId,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
        [(inst, o[0], o[1], o[2], o[3], o[4], o[5]) for o in batch]
    )
    cur.execute(f"""
        DELETE FROM ohlcv_{tf}
        WHERE instId=?
          AND ts NOT IN (
            SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_{tf}
            WHERE instId=?
            ORDER BY ts DESC
            LIMIT {MAX_ROWS}
          )
    """, (inst, inst))
    con.commit()
    con.close()

def sync_inst_tf(inst, tf):
    inst_ccxt = to_bitget_symbol(inst)
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    ts_last = last_ts(con, tf, inst)
    con.close()

    if ts_last is None:
        data = ex.fetch_ohlcv(inst_ccxt, tf, limit=INIT)
        upsert_batch(tf, inst, data)
        return

    data = ex.fetch_ohlcv(inst_ccxt, tf, since=ts_last + 1, limit=150)
    upsert_batch(tf, inst, data)

def main():
    ensure_schema()
    insts = load_universe()
    for inst in insts:
        for tf in TF_LIST:
            try:
                sync_inst_tf(inst, tf)
                time.sleep(0.25)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[OA][{inst}][{tf}] WARN: {e}")
    print("[OA] ✅ Multi-TF sync to oa.db")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OB_collect.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, time, sqlite3, logging, traceback
import ccxt
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
UDB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect.log"

# ---------------- LOG ----------------
logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s OB_COLLECT %(levelname)s %(message)s",
)
def log(msg):
    print(msg)
    logging.info(msg)

# ---------------- DATABASE ----------------
def db():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=3, check_same_thread=False)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

def load_universe():
    try:
        u = sqlite3.connect(UDB).execute("SELECT instId FROM universe").fetchall()
        return [row[0] for row in u]   # BTC/USDT
    except:
        return ["BTC/USDT"]

# ---------------- CCXT ----------------
def client():
    ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    return ex

# Convert instId → CCXT symbol
def to_symbol(inst):
    # BTC/USDT  → BTC/USDT:USDT   (Bitget future USDT perp)
    base, quote = inst.split("/")
    return f"{base}/{quote}:USDT"

# ---------------- SAVE OHLCV ----------------
def save_1m(conn, inst, rows):
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
        conn.execute("""
        INSERT INTO ohlcv_1m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
        VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        ON CONFLICT(instId,ts) DO UPDATE SET
            h = MAX(h, excluded.h),
            l = MIN(l, excluded.l),
            c = excluded.c,
            v = excluded.v;
        """, (inst.replace("/",""), ts, o,h,l,c,v))

    conn.commit()

def save_5m(conn, inst, rows):
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
        conn.execute("""
        INSERT INTO ohlcv_5m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
        VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        ON CONFLICT(instId,ts) DO UPDATE SET
            h = MAX(h, excluded.h),
            l = MIN(l, excluded.l),
            c = excluded.c,
            v = excluded.v;
        """, (inst.replace("/",""), ts, o,h,l,c,v))

    conn.commit()

# ---------------- TF3 = AGG TF1 ----------------
def rebuild_tf3(conn, inst):
    inst2 = inst.replace("/","")
    conn.execute(f"DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m WHERE instId='{inst2}'")

    conn.execute(f"""
    INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
    SELECT instId,
           ts - (ts % 180000) AS ts3,
           FIRST_VALUE(o) OVER w,
           MAX(h) OVER w,
           MIN(l) OVER w,
           LAST_VALUE(c) OVER w,
           SUM(v) OVER w
    FROM ohlcv_1m
    WHERE instId='{inst2}'
    WINDOW w AS (
        PARTITION BY instId, (ts - (ts % 180000))
        ORDER BY ts
        ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING
    )
    GROUP BY ts3;
    """)
    conn.commit()

# ---------------- PURGE ----------------
def purge(conn, inst):
    inst2 = inst.replace("/","")
    # TF1 450
    conn.execute(f"""
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m
    WHERE instId='{inst2}' AND ts NOT IN (
        SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_1m
        WHERE instId='{inst2}'
        ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 450
    );
    """)
    # TF5 150
    conn.execute(f"""
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
    WHERE instId='{inst2}' AND ts NOT IN (
        SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m
        WHERE instId='{inst2}'
        ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
    );
    """)
    # TF3 150
    conn.execute(f"""
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m
    WHERE instId='{inst2}' AND ts NOT IN (
        SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_3m
        WHERE instId='{inst2}'
        ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
    );
    """)
    conn.commit()

# ---------------- MAIN ----------------
def main():
    log("OB_COLLECT START")

    insts = load_universe()
    conn  = db()
    ex    = client()

    for inst in insts:
        try:
            symbol = to_symbol(inst)

            # ---- TF1 (450) ----
            ohlcv1 = ex.fetch_ohlcv(symbol, timeframe="1m", limit=450)
            save_1m(conn, inst, ohlcv1)

            # ---- TF5 (150) ----
            ohlcv5 = ex.fetch_ohlcv(symbol, timeframe="5m", limit=150)
            save_5m(conn, inst, ohlcv5)

            # ---- TF3 from TF1 ----
            rebuild_tf3(conn, inst)

            # ---- PURGE ----
            purge(conn, inst)

            log(f"OK {inst}")

        except Exception as e:
            log(f"ERR {inst} {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
            log(traceback.format_exc())

    log("OB_COLLECT END")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OB_collect_active.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# coding: utf-8
"""
SCALP - OB_COLLECT (incrémental)
→ Collecte les OHLCV Bitget pour TF 1m et 5m
→ Reconstitue TF 3m à partir de TF1
→ N'insère que les chandelles manquantes
→ Stocke dans ob.db
"""

import os, sys, time, logging, sqlite3, datetime
import ccxt

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect.log"
EXCHANGE = ccxt.bitget()

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG,
                    level=logging.INFO,
                    format="%(asctime)s OB_COLLECT %(levelname)s %(message)s")

# --- INIT DB ---------------------------------------------------------------
def init_db():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    for tf in ("1m", "3m", "5m"):
        cur.execute(f"""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_{tf} (
            instId TEXT NOT NULL,
            ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
            open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, vol REAL,
            PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
        );
        """)
    conn.commit()
    return conn

# --- FETCH OHLCV -----------------------------------------------------------
def fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=None, limit=200):
    try:
        ohlcv = EXCHANGE.fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=since, limit=limit)
        return [(inst, int(c[0]), c[1], c[2], c[3], c[4], c[5]) for c in ohlcv]
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"{inst} {tf} fetch error: {e}")
        return []

# --- BUILD 3M --------------------------------------------------------------
def rebuild_3m(cur):
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM feat_3m;")
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO feat_3m(instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol)
        SELECT instId,
               (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts,
               FIRST_VALUE(open) OVER w AS open,
               MAX(high) OVER w AS high,
               MIN(low) OVER w AS low,
               LAST_VALUE(close) OVER w AS close,
               SUM(vol) OVER w AS vol
        FROM feat_1m
        WINDOW w AS (PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000) ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING)
        GROUP BY instId, (ts/180000)
        ORDER BY instId, ts;
    """)

# --- MAIN LOOP -------------------------------------------------------------
def collect_all():
    conn = init_db()
    cur = conn.cursor()

    insts = [
        "BTC/USDT", "ETH/USDT", "SOL/USDT", "LTC/USDT", "BNB/USDT",
        "XRP/USDT", "DOGE/USDT", "ADA/USDT", "DOT/USDT", "LINK/USDT",
        "FIL/USDT", "ICP/USDT", "ATOM/USDT", "TRX/USDT", "AAVE/USDT",
        "BCH/USDT", "ETC/USDT", "UNI/USDT", "XLM/USDT", "XTZ/USDT"
    ]

    total_inserted = 0
    logging.info("start")

    for inst in insts:
        for tf in ("1m", "5m"):
            cur.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_{tf} WHERE instId=?", (inst,))
            ts_max = cur.fetchone()[0]
            since = ts_max + 60_000 if ts_max else None
            rows = fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=since, limit=450 if not ts_max else 2)
            if not rows:
                continue
            cur.executemany(f"""
                INSERT OR IGNORE INTO feat_{tf}(instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
            """, rows)
            total_inserted += len(rows)

    rebuild_3m(cur)
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    logging.info(f"done: {total_inserted} rows inserted.")

# --- ENTRYPOINT ------------------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        collect_all()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"FATAL: {e}")

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks.py -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# --- SCALP - TICKS COLLECTOR (Bitget Futures v2 WS) ---
# Inputs:  u.db (universe active=1)
# Outputs: t.db (ticks, ticks_hist, v_ticks_latest)
#
# WebSocket public Futures v2: wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public
# Maintient ticks temps réel, reconnecte automatiquement,
# logue tout, idempotent, conforme guide IA.

from __future__ import annotations
import argparse, asyncio, json, logging, sqlite3, sys, time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, List

DB_T = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
DB_U = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOGF = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/t_ticks.log"
WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

# --- LOGGING ---------------------------------------------------
def setup_logging() -> None:
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.INFO,
        format="%(asctime)s T_TICKS %(levelname)s %(message)s",
        handlers=[
            logging.FileHandler(LOGF),
            logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
        ],
        force=True,
    )

# --- SQLITE ----------------------------------------------------
def connect_db(path: str) -> sqlite3.Connection:
    con = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return con

SCHEMA_SQL = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
  instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  lastPr REAL,
  ts_ms INTEGER
);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks_hist(
  instId TEXT,
  lastPr REAL,
  ts_ms INTEGER,
  PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts_ms)
);
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
  t.instId,
  t.lastPr,
  t.ts_ms,
  strftime('%H:%M:%S', t.ts_ms/1000, 'unixepoch','localtime') AS hms,
  printf('%02d:%02d:%02d',
     ((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts_ms)/1000)/3600,
     (((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts_ms)/1000)%3600)/60,
     ((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts_ms)/1000)%60) AS age_hms
FROM ticks t
ORDER BY t.instId;
"""

def migrate(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    conn.executescript(SCHEMA_SQL)

def upsert_tick(db_t: str, instId: str, price: float, ts_ms: int) -> None:
    con = connect_db(db_t)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.execute(
        "INSERT INTO ticks_hist(instId,lastPr,ts_ms) VALUES(?,?,?) "
        "ON CONFLICT(instId,ts_ms) DO NOTHING;",
        (instId, price, ts_ms),
    )
    cur.execute(
        "INSERT INTO ticks(instId,lastPr,ts_ms) VALUES(?,?,?) "
        "ON CONFLICT(instId) DO UPDATE SET lastPr=excluded.lastPr, ts_ms=excluded.ts_ms;",
        (instId, price, ts_ms),
    )
    con.commit()
    con.close()

# --- UNIVERSE --------------------------------------------------
def load_universe(db_u: str) -> List[str]:
    con = connect_db(db_u)
    cur = con.cursor()
    try:
        insts = [r[0] for r in cur.execute(
            "SELECT instId FROM universe WHERE active=1 ORDER BY instId;"
        ).fetchall()]
        if not insts:
            raise Exception
    except Exception:
        insts = [r[0] for r in cur.execute(
            "SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId;"
        ).fetchall()]
    con.close()
    return [s.replace("/", "").upper() for s in insts]

# --- SELF TEST -------------------------------------------------
def smoke_test() -> None:
    tmp = Path("/tmp/t_ticks_ws_test.db")
    if tmp.exists():
        tmp.unlink()
    con = connect_db(str(tmp))
    migrate(con)
    now_ms = int(time.time() * 1000)
    con.execute("INSERT INTO ticks VALUES(?,?,?)", ("TESTUSDT", 1.2345, now_ms))
    row = con.execute("SELECT instId FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId='TESTUSDT'").fetchone()
    assert row and row[0] == "TESTUSDT", "self-test failed"
    con.close()
    tmp.unlink(missing_ok=True)
    logging.info("SELF-TEST OK")

# --- WEBSOCKET HANDLER ----------------------------------------
async def run_ws(db_t: str, db_u: str) -> None:
    import websockets

    while True:
        insts = load_universe(db_u)
        if not insts:
            logging.warning("Aucun instrument actif → attente 5s")
            await asyncio.sleep(5)
            continue

        try:
            async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=None) as ws:
                subs = [
                    {"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"ticker","instId":inst}
                    for inst in insts
                ]
                msg_sub = {"op":"subscribe","args":subs}
                await ws.send(json.dumps(msg_sub))
                logging.info(f"Abonnement envoyé ({len(subs)} paires)")

                last_ping = time.time()

                while True:
                    try:
                        raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=25)
                    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                        # heartbeat toutes 20s
                        await ws.send(json.dumps({"op":"ping"}))
                        last_ping = time.time()
                        continue

                    msg = json.loads(raw)
                    if "action" not in msg:
                        continue
                    if msg["action"] not in ("snapshot","update"):
                        continue
                    data = msg.get("data", [])
                    for d in data:
                        inst = d.get("instId")
                        pr = d.get("lastPr") or d.get("last") or d.get("markPrice")
                        ts_ms = int(d.get("ts") or int(time.time()*1000))
                        if not inst or not pr:
                            continue
                        upsert_tick(db_t, inst, float(pr), ts_ms)
                    await asyncio.sleep(0)  # yield event loop

        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"WS error: {e} → reconnect dans 3s")
            await asyncio.sleep(3)

# --- MAIN ------------------------------------------------------
def parse(argv: List[str]) -> argparse.Namespace:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="SCALP - Ticks collector (Bitget Futures WS)")
    p.add_argument("--db-t", default=DB_T)
    p.add_argument("--db-u", default=DB_U)
    p.add_argument("--self-test", action="store_true")
    return p.parse_args(argv)

def main(argv: List[str]) -> int:
    setup_logging()
    args = parse(argv)
    if args.self_test:
        smoke_test()
        return 0

    con = connect_db(args.db_t)
    migrate(con)
    con.close()

    asyncio.run(run_ws(args.db_t, args.db_u))
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks_debug.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio, json, websockets, datetime, re

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"

# liste restreinte pour test
INSTRUMENTS = ["BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT"]

async def listen():
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        subs = []
        for inst in INSTRUMENTS:
            subs.append({
                "op": "subscribe",
                "args": [f"ticker:{inst}_UMCBL"]
            })
        for s in subs:
            await ws.send(json.dumps(s))
        print("Subscriptions sent:", subs)

        count = 0
        while True:
            msg = await ws.recv()
            ts = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"\n[{ts}] RAW:", msg[:200])  # tronqué si long

            # test parsing brut
            try:
                clean = re.search(r'\{.*\}', msg)
                obj = json.loads(clean.group(0)) if clean else None
                if obj:
                    ticker = obj.get("data", [{}])[0]
                    inst = ticker.get("symbol", "?")
                    last = ticker.get("last", "?")
                    print(f"→ Parsed {inst} = {last}")
            except Exception as e:
                print("⚠️ Parse error:", e)

            count += 1
            if count >= 5:
                break

asyncio.run(listen())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks_test_raw.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio, json, time, websockets

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
INSTRUMENTS = ["BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT"]

async def test():
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=None) as ws:
        subs = [{"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "ticker", "instId": i} for i in INSTRUMENTS]
        msg = {"op": "subscribe", "args": subs}
        await ws.send(json.dumps(msg))
        print("✅ Sent:", msg)

        async def pinger():
            while True:
                await asyncio.sleep(10)
                await ws.send('{"op":"ping"}')
        asyncio.create_task(pinger())

        while True:
            raw = await ws.recv()
            ts = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"\n[{ts}] RAW →", raw[:250])

            try:
                data = json.loads(raw)
                if "data" in data:
                    for d in data["data"]:
                        inst = d.get("instId")
                        pr   = d.get("lastPr")
                        if inst and pr:
                            print(f"→ Parsed {inst} = {pr}")
            except Exception as e:
                print("⚠️ Parse error:", e)

asyncio.run(test())

import ccxt, sqlite3

DBU = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
TOP = 20

exchange = ccxt.bitget()
markets = exchange.load_markets()

perps = []
for s,info in markets.items():
    if info.get('swap',False) and info['quote'] == 'USDT':
        inst = s.replace(":USDT","")  # -> BTC/USDT:USDT → BTC/USDT
        perps.append(inst)

perps = perps[:TOP]

con = sqlite3.connect(DBU, timeout=5)
con.execute("DELETE FROM universe;")
for inst in perps:
    con.execute("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe(instId) VALUES (?)", (inst,))
con.commit()
con.close()

print("[U] OK :", perps)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/b_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time
from datetime import datetime

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_B = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_T = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

def get_ctx():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_A) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT instId, ctx FROM v_ctx_latest WHERE ctx IN ('bullish','bearish','range');")
        return cur.fetchall()

def get_last_tick(inst):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_T) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT lastPr, ts_ms FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1;", (inst,))
        r = cur.fetchone()
    if not r:
        return None, None, None, None
    pr, ts_ms = r
    ts_s = ts_ms / 1000
    hms = datetime.fromtimestamp(ts_s).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
    delta = round(time.time() - ts_s, 1)
    return pr, ts_s, hms, delta

def get_last_signal(inst):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_B) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT ts FROM signals WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1;", (inst,))
        r = cur.fetchone()
    if not r:
        return None, None, None
    ts = float(r[0])
    hms = datetime.fromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
    delta = round(time.time() - ts, 1)
    return ts, hms, delta

def dash():
    print(f"===== DASH {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')} =====")
    for inst, ctx in get_ctx():
        pr, ts_tick, hms_tick, delta_tick = get_last_tick(inst)
        ts_sig, hms_sig, delta_sig = get_last_signal(inst)

        delta = "-"
        if ts_tick and ts_sig:
            delta = round(ts_tick - ts_sig, 1)

        flag = "⚠️" if delta_tick and delta_tick > 5 else "✅"
        print(f"{inst:<10} | ctx={ctx:<8} | price={pr or '-':<10} | "
              f"tick={hms_tick or '-':>8} | sig={hms_sig or '-':>8} | "
              f"Δ={delta:<6} | {flag}")
    print("=" * 90)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    while True:
        try:
            dash()
            time.sleep(3)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            break
        except Exception as e:
            print("B_DASH ERROR:", e)
            time.sleep(5)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    print(f"[BUDGET] Event logged: {instId} → {event}")

def main():
    while True:
        print("[BUDGET] Updating exposure / allocation")
        bus_notify("ALL", "BUDGET_UPDATED")
        time.sleep(20)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget_updater.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, logging, sys
from pathlib import Path

DB_BUDGET  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db")
DB_OPENER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db")
DB_CLOSER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db")
DB_REC     = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db")
LOG        = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/budget.log"

# -----------------------------------------------------
def setup_logging():
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.INFO,
        format="%(asctime)s BUDGET %(levelname)s %(message)s",
        handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG), logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)],
        force=True,
    )

# -----------------------------------------------------
def connect(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return c

# -----------------------------------------------------
def get_margin_engaged(con_o):
    """Somme de la marge estimée sur les positions ouvertes/pending."""
    try:
        res = con_o.execute("""
            SELECT SUM(entry * qty / leverage)
            FROM trades_open_init
            WHERE status IN ('pending','open');
        """).fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_pnl_real(con_r):
    """Somme du PnL réalisé total depuis l’historique."""
    try:
        res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl_net) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        if res is None:
            res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_capital_initial(con_b):
    """Capital initial du budget (si non encore présent, crée 1000 USDT)."""
    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS budget_state(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id=1),
            balance REAL DEFAULT 1000.0,
            margin REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            pnl_real REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            ts_update INTEGER
        );
    """)
    con_b.commit()
    row = con_b.execute("SELECT balance FROM budget_state WHERE id=1;").fetchone()
    if not row:
        con_b.execute("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO budget_state(id,balance,margin,pnl_real,ts_update) VALUES (1,1000.0,0.0,0.0,strftime('%s','now'));")
        con_b.commit()
        return 1000.0
    return float(row[0])

# -----------------------------------------------------
def update_budget():
    con_b = connect(DB_BUDGET)
    con_o = connect(DB_OPENER)
    con_r = connect(DB_REC)

    capital = get_capital_initial(con_b)
    margin  = get_margin_engaged(con_o)
    pnl_real = get_pnl_real(con_r)

    new_balance = capital + pnl_real
    ts_now = int(time.time())

    con_b.execute("""
        UPDATE budget_state
        SET balance=?, margin=?, pnl_real=?, ts_update=?
        WHERE id=1;
    """, (new_balance, margin, pnl_real, ts_now))
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_budget_overview AS
        SELECT
            ROUND(balance,4) AS balance,
            ROUND(margin,4)  AS margin,
            ROUND(pnl_real,4) AS pnl_real,
            datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
        FROM budget_state;
    """)
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.close(); con_o.close(); con_r.close()
    logging.info(f"MAJ budget → balance={new_balance:.2f} margin={margin:.2f} pnl_real={pnl_real:.2f}")

# -----------------------------------------------------
def main(_):
    setup_logging()
    logging.info("Budget updater started ✓")
    try:
        update_budget()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.exception(f"Erreur mise à jour budget: {e}")
        raise SystemExit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/bus_utils.py -----
import sqlite3, json, time
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

DB_PATH = "/opt/scalp/project/data/bus.db"

def get_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH, timeout=2, isolation_level=None)
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return conn

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Send a message from one module to another
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_send(source: str, dest: str, stage: str, instId: str, payload: Dict):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO bus (stage, source, dest, instId, payload)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    """, (stage, source, dest, instId, json.dumps(payload)))
    conn.close()

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Receive unread messages for a given destination + optional stage
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_recv(dest: str, stage: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Dict]:
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    if stage:
        rows = cur.execute("""
            SELECT * FROM bus
            WHERE dest=? AND stage=? AND ack=0
            ORDER BY id ASC
        """, (dest, stage)).fetchall()
    else:
        rows = cur.execute("""
            SELECT * FROM bus
            WHERE dest=? AND ack=0
            ORDER BY id ASC
        """, (dest,)).fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return [dict(r) for r in rows]

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Mark a message as processed
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_ack(msg_id: int):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("UPDATE bus SET ack=1 WHERE id=?", (msg_id,))
    conn.close()

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Clean acknowledged messages older than N days
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_clean(days: int = 1):
    cutoff = int((time.time() - days * 86400) * 1000)
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM bus WHERE ack=1 AND ts < ?", (cutoff,))
    conn.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, random

def bus_notify(instId, event):

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/closer_finalize.py -----
import sqlite3, time, logging

DB_FOLLOW = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_CLOSER = "/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_REC = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"
DB_BUDGET = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"
DB_TICKS = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s CLOSER FIX %(levelname)s %(message)s")

def get_last_price(instId):
    """Récupère le dernier prix connu depuis t.db"""
    try:
        with sqlite3.connect(DB_TICKS) as ct:
            cur = ct.cursor()
            cur.execute("SELECT lastPr FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1;", (instId,))
            row = cur.fetchone()
            return float(row[0]) if row else None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"{instId}: erreur lecture ticks → {e}")
        return None

def finalize_closures():
    con_f = sqlite3.connect(DB_FOLLOW)
    con_c = sqlite3.connect(DB_CLOSER)
    con_r = sqlite3.connect(DB_REC)
    con_b = sqlite3.connect(DB_BUDGET)

    cur_f = con_f.cursor()
    cur_c = con_c.cursor()
    cur_r = con_r.cursor()
    cur_b = con_b.cursor()

    rows = cur_f.execute("""
        SELECT instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason_close,
               score_U, score_A, score_B, ts_open, ts_update
        FROM trades_follow
        WHERE status='to_close'
    """).fetchall()

    if not rows:
        logging.info("Aucune position à finaliser.")
        return

    for instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason, sU, sA, sB, ts_open, ts_close in rows:
        if last is None:
            last = get_last_price(instId)
            if last is None:
                last = entry
                logging.warning(f"{instId}: aucun prix disponible → fallback entry={entry}")
            else:
                logging.info(f"{instId}: récupéré last depuis ticks = {last}")

        pnl = round((last - entry) * qty * (1 if side == 'buy' else -1), 6)
        logging.info(f"→ CLOSE {instId} {side} pnl={pnl} reason={reason}")

        cur_c.execute("""
            INSERT INTO positions_closed(instId,side,entry,exit,qty,pnl,sl,tp,ts_open,ts_close,reason_exit,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,qty,pnl,0,0,ts_open,ts_close,reason,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_r.execute("""
            INSERT INTO trades_recorded(instId,side,entry,exit,pnl,reason_exit,ts_open,ts_close,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,pnl,reason,ts_open,ts_close,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_b.execute("""
            INSERT INTO ledger(src,instId,type,amount,ts)
            VALUES ('closer',?, 'pnl_real', ?, strftime('%s','now')*1000)
        """, (instId, pnl))

        cur_f.execute("UPDATE trades_follow SET status='closed' WHERE instId=?;", (instId,))

    con_c.commit()
    con_r.commit()
    con_b.commit()
    con_f.commit()
    logging.info(f"✓ {len(rows)} clôture(s) finalisée(s).")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    finalize_closures()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/diag_schema.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
diag_schema.py : validation stricte des colonnes contre schema_ref.sql
- Sensible au contexte DB (opener.db / follower.db / closer.db / recorder.db)
- Ignore sqlite_sequence
- Nettoie les commentaires '-- ...' et '/* ... */' avant parsing
- Code retour: 0 si OK, 1 si divergences, 2 si schema_ref absent
Logs: /opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_schema.log
"""
from __future__ import annotations
import re, sys, sqlite3, logging
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data")
SCHEMA_FILE = DATA / "schema_ref.sql"
DBS = [
    ("opener.db",   DATA / "opener.db"),
    ("follower.db", DATA / "follower.db"),
    ("closer.db",   DATA / "closer.db"),
    ("recorder.db", DATA / "recorder.db"),
]

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler("/opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_schema.log"),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
    ],
)

SectionMap = Dict[str, Dict[str, List[str]]]  # {db_name: {table: [cols...]}}

def _strip_sql_comments(sql: str) -> str:
    sql = re.sub(r"/\*.*?\*/", "", sql, flags=re.S)       # /* ... */
    # Retire les lignes de commentaire -- (en conservant les marqueurs de section)
    cleaned_lines = []
    for line in sql.splitlines():
        if line.strip().startswith("-- ---"):  # garde sections
            cleaned_lines.append(line)
            continue
        if line.strip().startswith("--"):
            continue
        cleaned_lines.append(line)
    return "\n".join(cleaned_lines)

def _split_statements(sql: str) -> List[str]:
    out, buf, depth = [], [], 0
    for ch in sql:
        if ch == "(":
            depth += 1
        elif ch == ")":
            depth = max(depth - 1, 0)
        buf.append(ch)
        if ch == ";" and depth == 0:
            out.append("".join(buf).strip())
            buf = []
    tail = "".join(buf).strip()
    if tail:
        out.append(tail)
    return out

def _extract_cols_from_create(create_sql: str) -> Tuple[str, List[str]]:
    m = re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+(\w+)\s*\((.*)\)\s*;?$", create_sql.strip())
    if not m:
        return "", []
    tname = m.group(1)
    body = m.group(2)

    # Découpe par virgules au niveau 0
    cols_defs: List[str] = []
    token, depth = "", 0
    for ch in body:
        if ch == "(":
            depth += 1
        elif ch == ")":
            depth = max(depth - 1, 0)
        if ch == "," and depth == 0:
            t = token.strip()
            if t:
                cols_defs.append(t)
            token = ""
        else:
            token += ch
    if token.strip():
        cols_defs.append(token.strip())

    cols: List[str] = []
    for cdef in cols_defs:
        s = cdef.strip()
        # ignore contraintes de table
        if re.match(r"(?is)PRIMARY\s+KEY|UNIQUE|CHECK|FOREIGN\s+KEY|CONSTRAINT", s):
            continue
        # prends le premier token comme nom de colonne
        parts = s.split()
        if parts:
            col = parts[0]
            # filtre d'éventuels artefacts comme "--"
            if col != "--":
                cols.append(col)
    return tname, cols

def parse_schema_by_db(schema_text: str) -> SectionMap:
    """
    Parse schema_ref.sql en respectant les sections:
    -- --- opener.db ---   etc.
    Retour: { 'opener.db': {'table': [cols...] , ...}, ... }
    """
    sections: SectionMap = {}
    current = None
    buf = []

    # On garde les sections pour orienter les CREATE TABLE qui suivent
    for line in schema_text.splitlines():
        m = re.match(r"--\s*---\s*([A-Za-z0-9_\.]+)\s*---", line)
        if m:
            # flush précédent
            if current and buf:
                chunk = "\n".join(buf)
                for stmt in _split_statements(chunk):
                    if re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+", stmt):
                        tname, cols = _extract_cols_from_create(stmt)
                        if tname and tname != "sqlite_sequence":
                            sections.setdefault(current, {})[tname] = cols
                buf = []
            current = m.group(1)
            sections.setdefault(current, {})
            continue
        buf.append(line)

    # flush final
    if current and buf:
        chunk = "\n".join(buf)
        for stmt in _split_statements(chunk):
            if re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+", stmt):
                tname, cols = _extract_cols_from_create(stmt)
                if tname and tname != "sqlite_sequence":
                    sections.setdefault(current, {})[tname] = cols

    return sections

def fetch_db_cols(db_path: Path) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
    out: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
    if not db_path.exists() or db_path.stat().st_size == 0:
        return out
    con = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))
    try:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'")
        for (tname,) in cur.fetchall():
            try:
                cur.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({tname})")
                cols = [r[1] for r in cur.fetchall()]
                out[tname] = cols
            except sqlite3.DatabaseError:
                continue
    finally:
        con.close()
    return out

def main() -> int:
    if not SCHEMA_FILE.exists():
        logging.error("schema_ref.sql introuvable")
        return 2

    raw = SCHEMA_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    cleaned = _strip_sql_comments(raw)
    ref_by_db = parse_schema_by_db(cleaned)

    global_ok = True
    for db_name, db_path in DBS:
        got = fetch_db_cols(db_path)
        if not got:
            logging.warning(f"{db_name}: DB absente ou vide")
            continue

        logging.info(f"--- {db_name} ---")
        ref_tables = ref_by_db.get(db_name, {})

        # compare uniquement les tables présentes dans la REF pour CETTE DB
        for tname, cols_ref in ref_tables.items():
            if tname not in got:
                # table attendue dans cette DB mais absente → signaler
                logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → table manquante")
                global_ok = False
                continue
            cols_got = got[tname]
            miss = [c for c in cols_ref if c not in cols_got]
            extra = [c for c in cols_got if c not in cols_ref]
            if miss or extra:
                global_ok = False
                if miss:
                    logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → colonnes manquantes: {', '.join(miss)}")
                if extra:
                    logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → colonnes en trop: {', '.join(extra)}")

        logging.info(f"{db_name}: CHECK terminé")

    if global_ok:
        print("✅ diag_schema: schéma conforme aux colonnes de schema_ref.sql (par DB)")
        return 0
    else:
        print("❌ diag_schema: divergences détectées (voir logs)")
        return 1

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/follower.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, random, sys, traceback

# force stdout à flusher chaque print immédiatement
sys.stdout.reconfigure(line_buffering=True)

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"

def get_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()
        cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        print(f"[FOLLOWER] Event logged: {instId} → {event}", flush=True)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[FOLLOWER ERR][bus_notify] {e}", flush=True)

def main():
    insts = ["BTC/USDT", "ETH/USDT", "ADA/USDT", "SOL/USDT", "XRP/USDT"]
    print("[FOLLOWER] Service started.", flush=True)
    cycle = 0
    while True:
        try:
            cycle += 1
            inst = random.choice(insts)
            pnl = round(random.uniform(-1.5, 1.5), 3)
            print(f"[FOLLOWER] {cycle:04d}  FOLLOW {inst}  pnl={pnl:+.3f}", flush=True)
            bus_notify(inst, "FOLLOW_DONE")
            time.sleep(5)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n[FOLLOWER] stopped manually.", flush=True)
            sys.exit(0)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[FOLLOWER ERR][main] {e}", flush=True)
            traceback.print_exc()
            time.sleep(2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gen_schema_ref.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# -------- CONFIG --------
DATA_DIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"
OUT="${DATA_DIR}/schema_ref.sql"

# -------- INIT --------
{
  echo "-- === SCHEMA GLOBAL SCALP ==="
  echo "-- Généré le $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
  echo
} > "$OUT"

# -------- EXTRACTION COMPLÈTE --------
for DB in opener.db follower.db closer.db recorder.db; do
  DB_PATH="${DATA_DIR}/${DB}"
  echo "-- --- $DB ---" >> "$OUT"
  if [[ -f "$DB_PATH" ]]; then
    # Sortie complète des tables et vues
    sqlite3 "$DB_PATH" "SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type IN ('table','view') AND sql NOT NULL ORDER BY name;" \
      >> "$OUT" 2>/dev/null || true
    echo >> "$OUT"
  else
    echo "-- (absent) $DB" >> "$OUT"
    echo >> "$OUT"
  fi
done

echo "-- === FIN ===" >> "$OUT"
echo "✅ Schéma complet sauvegardé dans $OUT"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3
import logging
import time
import os

# === chemins ===
ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project/data"
DB_G = f"{ROOT}/gest.db"
DB_B = f"{ROOT}/b.db"
LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/gest.log"

# === logging ===
logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
)

# === UID stable ===
def make_uid(instId, side, ts_signal):
    return f"T{ts_signal}_{instId.replace('/','')}_{side}"

# === import signaux depuis B ===
def copy_signals_to_trades(limit=500):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_B) as src, sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as dst:
        src.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
        dst.row_factory = sqlite3.Row

        # Signaux nouveaux uniquement
        rows = src.execute("""
            SELECT b.instId, b.side, b.reason, b.price, b.atr, b.score_B, b.ts_signal,
                   COALESCE(c.ctx,'range') AS ctx
            FROM v_opener_for_gest b
            LEFT JOIN gest.trades_all g
                ON g.instId=b.instId AND g.side=b.side AND g.ts_signal=b.ts_signal
            LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c ON c.instId=b.instId
            WHERE b.price>0 AND g.trade_uid IS NULL
            ORDER BY b.ts_signal DESC
            LIMIT ?
        """, (limit,)).fetchall()

        n_new = 0
        for r in rows:
            t_uid = make_uid(r["instId"], r["side"], r["ts_signal"])
            try:
                dst.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO trades_all(
                        trade_uid, instId, side, reason, ctx,
                        score_B, atr, price, ts_signal,
                        state, ts_create
                    ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,'NEW',strftime('%s','now')*1000)
                """, (
                    t_uid, r["instId"], r["side"], r["reason"], r["ctx"],
                    r["score_B"], r["atr"], r["price"], r["ts_signal"]
                ))
                n_new += 1
            except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
                continue

        dst.commit()
        if n_new > 0:
            logging.info(f"SYNC {n_new} nouveaux signaux ajoutés")
        return n_new

# === budget ===
def update_budget():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as con:
        pnl_total = con.execute("""
            SELECT COALESCE(SUM(pnl_real),0)
            FROM trades_all
            WHERE state IN ('ACTIVE','CLOSING','CLOSED','RECORDED')
        """).fetchone()[0]
        base_balance = 1000.0
        balance = base_balance + pnl_total
        con.execute("""
            UPDATE budget_state
            SET balance=?, equity=?, margin=0,
                ts_update=strftime('%s','now')*1000
            WHERE id=1
        """, (balance, balance))
        con.commit()
        logging.info(f"BUDGET mis à jour → balance={balance:.2f}")

# === initialisation ===
def init_budget():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as con:
        con.execute("""
            INSERT OR IGNORE INTO budget_state(id,balance,equity,margin,ts_update)
            VALUES (1,1000,1000,0,strftime('%s','now')*1000)
        """)
        con.commit()

# === boucle principale ===
def main():
    logging.info("GEST pipeline actif (b→gest)")
    init_budget()
    while True:
        try:
            added = copy_signals_to_trades()
            if added > 0:
                update_budget()
            time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"GEST loop error: {e}")
            time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest_bus_collector.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import sqlite3, json, time, logging, os

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project/data"
SRC = {
  "b": f"{ROOT}/b.db",
  "opener": f"{ROOT}/opener.db",
  "closer": f"{ROOT}/closer.db",
}
GEST_DB = f"{ROOT}/gest.db"
LOG_FILE = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/gest_bus.log"

os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(LOG_FILE), exist_ok=True)
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO,
                    format="%(asctime)s GEST_BUS %(levelname)s %(message)s")

def connect(db_path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(db_path, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def json_load(s):
    try: return json.loads(s) if s else {}
    except: return {}

def process_row(gcur, row, source):
    inst, event, ts = row["instId"], row["event"], row["ts"]
    payload = json_load(row["payload"] or "{}")
    gcur.execute("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO bus_out(id, src, instId, event, payload, ts, ack) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,1);",
                 (row["id"], source, inst, event, row["payload"], ts))
    if event in ("NEW_SIGNAL","NEW_TRIGGER"):
        gcur.execute("""INSERT INTO signals_in(instId, side, reason, score, confidence, ctx, ts)
                        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?);""",
                     (inst, payload.get("side"), payload.get("reason"),
                      float(payload.get("score",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("confidence",0) or 0),
                      payload.get("ctx"), ts))
    elif event == "OPEN_DONE":
        gcur.execute("""INSERT INTO trades_all(instId, side, reason, entry, sl, tp, qty, ts_open, status)
                        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,'open');""",
                     (inst, payload.get("side"), payload.get("reason"),
                      float(payload.get("entry",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("sl",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("tp",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("qty",0) or 0), ts))
    elif event == "CLOSE_DONE":
        gcur.execute("""UPDATE trades_all
                        SET pnl=?, ts_close=?, status='closed'
                        WHERE instId=? AND status='open'
                        ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 1;""",
                     (float(payload.get("pnl",0) or 0), ts, inst))

def main():
    logging.info("GEST_BUS démarré")
    gest = connect(GEST_DB); gcur = gest.cursor()
    sources = {n: connect(p) for n,p in SRC.items() if os.path.exists(p)}
    cursors = {n: c.cursor() for n,c in sources.items()}

    while True:
        try:
            total = 0
            for name, cur in cursors.items():
                cur.execute("SELECT id, src, instId, event, payload, ts FROM bus_out WHERE ack=0 ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 200;")
                rows = cur.fetchall()
                for r in rows:
                    process_row(gcur, r, name)
                    cur.execute("UPDATE bus_out SET ack=1 WHERE id=?;", (r["id"],))
                total += len(rows)
            if total:
                gest.commit()
                for c in sources.values(): c.commit()
                logging.info(f"{total} événements traités.")
            time.sleep(2)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"loop error: {e}")
            time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, os, time
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=2)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def latest_events(cur, limit=15):
    rows = cur.execute("""
        SELECT src, instId, event,
               datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
        FROM bus_events
        ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT ?;
    """, (limit,)).fetchall()
    return rows

def summary(cur):
    rows = cur.execute("""
        SELECT src,
               COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE event LIKE '%DONE%') AS done,
               COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE event LIKE 'NEW%') AS new,
               MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_ts
        FROM bus_events
        GROUP BY src
        ORDER BY src;
    """).fetchall()
    return rows

def main():
    os.system("clear")
    print("===== SCALP BUS DASHBOARD (GEST) =====")
    print(f"{datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print()

    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()

        srows = summary(cur)
        print("--- SUMMARY ---")
        if not srows:
            print("No data yet.")
        else:
            print(f"{'SRC':<10}{'NEW':>6}{'DONE':>8}{'LAST_EVENT':>22}")
            for r in srows:
                print(f"{r['src']:<10}{r['new']:>6}{r['done']:>8}{r['last_ts']:>22}")
        print()

        rows = latest_events(cur)
        print("--- LATEST EVENTS ---")
        print(f"{'SRC':<10}{'INSTID':<15}{'EVENT':<15}{'TIMESTAMP':>22}")
        for r in rows:
            print(f"{r['src']:<10}{r['instId']:<15}{r['event']:<15}{r['ts_local']:>22}")

        conn.close()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERR] {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        while True:
            main()
            time.sleep(2)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n[GEST DASH] stopped.")

  'T' || strftime('%s','now') || '_' || REPLACE(instId,'/','') || '_' || side || '_' || hex(randomblob(2)),
  instId,
  side,
  reason,
  'unknown',
  score_B,

  ts_signal
FROM bdb.signals_B

  trade_uid,
  instId,
  side,

FROM signals_in;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/health_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, sys
from datetime import datetime

DB_O = "/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_F = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_BUDGET = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"

def connect(db):
    con = sqlite3.connect(db)
    con.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return con

def print_table(title, rows):
    print(f"\n--- {title} ---")
    if not rows:
        print("(vide)")
        return
    headers = rows[0].keys()
    print(" | ".join(headers))
    for r in rows:
        print(" | ".join(str(r[k]) for k in headers))

def main():
    print(f"===== PIPELINE HEALTH {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')} =====")
    co = connect(DB_O)
    cf = connect(DB_F)
    cb = connect(DB_BUDGET)

    print_table("OPEN POSITIONS (opener)", co.execute(
        "SELECT instId, side, status, margin_used FROM trades_open_init ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 10;"
    ).fetchall())

    print_table("FOLLOW POSITIONS (follower)", cf.execute(
        "SELECT instId, side, status, pnl FROM trades_follow ORDER BY ts_update DESC LIMIT 10;"
    ).fetchall())

    print_table("BUDGET OVERVIEW", cb.execute(
        "SELECT * FROM v_budget_overview;"
    ).fetchall())

    co.close(); cf.close(); cb.close()
    print("\n===== END DASH =====")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import sqlite3

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

def init_db():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_5m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_15m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_30m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ctx_a (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        p_buy REAL,
        p_hold REAL,
        p_sell REAL,
        score REAL,
        ctx TEXT
    );
    """)

    con.commit()
    con.close()
    print("[INIT_DB] OK – A DB ready")
